Universal Containers utilizes opportunities and a custom object called Detailed_Sales__c. The company would like to roll sales metrics up to an opportunity for only Detailed_Sales__c records that have their picklist status set to Active. What is the recommended method for the app builder to achieve this request?


Universal Containers å…¬å¸ä½¿ç”¨ã€Œæ©Ÿæœƒ (Opportunity)ã€å’Œä¸€å€‹åç‚º Detailed_Sales__c çš„è‡ªè¨‚ç‰©ä»¶ã€‚å…¬å¸å¸Œæœ›å°‡éŠ·å”®æŒ‡æ¨™åŒ¯ç¸½åˆ°ã€Œæ©Ÿæœƒã€ä¸Šï¼Œä½†åƒ…é™æ–¼ Detailed_Sales__c è¨˜éŒ„ä¸­é¸é …æ¸…å–® (picklist) ç‹€æ…‹è¨­å®šç‚ºã€Œå•Ÿç”¨ (Active)ã€çš„è¨˜éŒ„ã€‚å°æ–¼æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€… (App Builder) ä¾†èªªï¼Œå»ºè­°ç”¨å“ªç¨®æ–¹æ³•ä¾†å¯¦ç¾é€™å€‹éœ€æ±‚ï¼Ÿ

åœ¨çˆ¶ç‰©ä»¶å’Œå­ç‰©ä»¶ä¹‹é–“å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹ä¸»å¾å¼é—œä¿‚ (master-detail relationship)ï¼Œä¸¦ä½¿ç”¨ä¸€å€‹å¯ä»¥æ ¹æ“šç‹€æ…‹æ¬„ä½é€²è¡Œç¯©é¸çš„ç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½ (roll-up summary field)ã€‚

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): B

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
Create a master-detail relationship between the parent and child object with a roll-up summary field that filters on the status field is the recommended method for the app builder to achieve the request. According to the Salesforce documentation, "Roll-up summary fields calculate values from related records, such as those in a master-detail relationship." A roll-up summary field can filter on a field value of the child records and sum up only those records that match the criteria.

Which two solutions prevent a formula field from being referenced by a Roll-Up Summary Field? (Choose 2 answers)


å“ªå…©å€‹è§£æ±ºæ–¹æ¡ˆæœƒé˜»æ­¢å…¬å¼æ¬„ä½è¢«ã€Œç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½ (Roll-Up Summary Field)ã€å¼•ç”¨ï¼Ÿ(é¸æ“‡ 2 å€‹ç­”æ¡ˆ)


A. A cross-object workflow updating a field referenced by the formula field
Â Â Â Â Â 

è·¨ç‰©ä»¶å·¥ä½œæµç¨‹æ›´æ–°äº†å…¬å¼æ¬„ä½æ‰€å¼•ç”¨çš„æ¬„ä½ã€‚

B. A cross-object field reference in the formula field
Â Â Â Â Â 

å…¬å¼æ¬„ä½ä¸­æœ‰è·¨ç‰©ä»¶çš„æ¬„ä½å¼•ç”¨ã€‚

C. The CASE() function in the formula field
Â Â Â Â Â 

å…¬å¼æ¬„ä½ä¸­æœ‰ CASE() å‡½æ•¸ã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): B, D

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
A formula field cannot be referenced by a roll-up summary field if it contains a cross-object field reference or a time-based function. A cross-object field reference is a reference to a field from a different object, such as Account.Name on a Contact object. A time-based function is a function that returns the current date or time, such as NOW() or TODAY().

The proposal has three custom objectsrelated to the Account object, one with a master-detail, and two that are not. Each of these objects has 15 fields they would like to summarize on the Account object. What are two considerations for this proposal? (Choose 2 answers)


ç‚ºäº†æé«˜æ¡ç”¨ç‡ï¼ŒUniversal Containers å…¬å¸æè­°å°å…¶ Salesforce è³‡æ–™æ¨¡å‹é€²è¡Œè®Šæ›´ï¼Œä»¥ä¾¿éŠ·å”®ä»£è¡¨æ›´å®¹æ˜“æŸ¥çœ‹é—œéµæŒ‡æ¨™ã€‚è©²ææ¡ˆæœ‰ä¸‰å€‹èˆ‡ã€Œå¸³æˆ¶ (Account)ã€ç‰©ä»¶ç›¸é—œçš„è‡ªè¨‚ç‰©ä»¶ï¼Œå…¶ä¸­ä¸€å€‹æ˜¯ä¸»å¾å¼é—œä¿‚ï¼Œå¦å¤–å…©å€‹ä¸æ˜¯ã€‚ä»–å€‘å¸Œæœ›åœ¨ã€Œå¸³æˆ¶ã€ç‰©ä»¶ä¸ŠåŒ¯ç¸½é€™ä¸‰å€‹ç‰©ä»¶ä¸­å„ 15 å€‹æ¬„ä½çš„è³‡æ–™ã€‚ å°æ–¼æ­¤ææ¡ˆï¼Œæœ‰å“ªå…©é …è€ƒé‡å› ç´ ï¼Ÿ(é¸æ“‡ 2 å€‹ç­”æ¡ˆ)


A. Roll-up summaries allow MAX, MIN, SUM, COUNT, and AVG.
Â Â Â Â Â 

ç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½å…è¨± MAXã€MINã€SUMã€COUNT å’Œ AVG å‡½æ•¸ã€‚

B. An object can have 20 object references.
Â Â Â Â Â 

ä¸€å€‹ç‰©ä»¶å¯ä»¥æœ‰ 20 å€‹ç‰©ä»¶å¼•ç”¨ã€‚

C. An object can have 25 roll-up summaries.
Â Â Â Â Â 

ä¸€å€‹ç‰©ä»¶å¯ä»¥æœ‰ 25 å€‹ç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½ã€‚

D. Roll-up summaries are limited to master-detail relationships.
Â Â Â Â Â 

ç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½åƒ…é™æ–¼ä¸»å¾å¼é—œä¿‚ã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): A, D

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
Roll-up summaries allow MAX, MIN, SUM, COUNT, and AVG functions on numeric fields from child records related by a master-detail relationship. Roll-up summaries are limited to master-detail relationships and cannot be used with lookup relationships. An object can have up to 40 roll-up summary fields, not 25.
ç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½å…è¨±å°é€éä¸»å¾å¼é—œä¿‚é—œè¯çš„å­è¨˜éŒ„ä¸­çš„æ•¸å­—æ¬„ä½ä½¿ç”¨ MAXã€MINã€SUMã€COUNT å’Œ AVG å‡½æ•¸ã€‚ç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½åƒ…é™æ–¼ä¸»å¾å¼é—œä¿‚ï¼Œä¸èƒ½èˆ‡æŸ¥è©¢é—œä¿‚ä¸€èµ·ä½¿ç”¨ã€‚ä¸€å€‹ç‰©ä»¶æœ€å¤šå¯ä»¥æœ‰ 40 å€‹ç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½ï¼Œè€Œä¸æ˜¯ 25 å€‹ã€‚

DreamMouse Realty æœ‰ä¸€å€‹å°å¸«è¨ˆç•«ï¼Œå°‡æœ‰ç¶“é©—çš„æˆ¿åœ°ç”¢ç¶“ç´€äººèˆ‡æ–°é€²ç¶“ç´€äººé…å°ã€‚æ¯ä½æœ‰ç¶“é©—çš„ç¶“ç´€äººå¯ä»¥æŒ‡å°ä¸€ä½æˆ–å¤šä½æ–°é€²ç¶“ç´€äººï¼Œè€Œæ¯ä½æ–°é€²ç¶“ç´€äººéƒ½å¿…é ˆåœ¨è©¦ç”¨æœŸå…§èˆ‡ä¸€ä½ä»–å€‘æ‰€å±¬çš„æœ‰ç¶“é©—çš„ç¶“ç´€äººåˆä½œã€‚ æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æ‡‰è¨­å®šå“ªç¨®é¡å‹çš„é—œä¿‚ä¾†æ»¿è¶³æ­¤è¦ç¯„ï¼Ÿ

é–“æ¥æŸ¥è©¢

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): D

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
Lookup is the type of relationship that would be set up to meet the specification. According to the Salesforce documentation, "A lookup relationship creates a loose association between objects. Universal Containers manages leads in a Lead qualification queue where sales reps can accept ownership of the Lead. Campaign members are required to have a sales owner. What validation rule should an app builder configure?


Universal Containers å…¬å¸åœ¨ä¸€å€‹ã€Œæ½›åœ¨å®¢æˆ¶è³‡æ ¼ä½‡åˆ—ã€ä¸­ç®¡ç†æ½›åœ¨å®¢æˆ¶ï¼ŒéŠ·å”®ä»£è¡¨å¯ä»¥åœ¨æ­¤æ¥å—æ½›åœ¨å®¢æˆ¶çš„æ‰€æœ‰æ¬Šã€‚ç³»çµ±è¦æ±‚ã€Œè¡ŒéŠ·æ´»å‹•æˆå“¡ (Campaign members)ã€å¿…é ˆæœ‰ä¸€å€‹éŠ·å”®è² è²¬äººã€‚æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æ‡‰è©²è¨­å®šä»€éº¼æ¨£çš„é©—è­‰è¦å‰‡ï¼Ÿ


A. AND(ISBLANK(Lead.Owner.Id))

B. NOT(ISNEW() && ISBLANK(Lead.Owner:Queue.Id))

C. AND(ISNEW(), ISBLANK(Lead.Owner:User.Id))

D. NOT(ISBLANK(Lead.Owner:Queue.Id))


é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): C

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The validation rule should be AND(ISNEW(), ISBLANK(Lead.Owner:User.Id)). This rule will prevent saving a new lead record if the owner is not a user. This will ensure that campaign members have a sales owner.
é©—è­‰è¦å‰‡æ‡‰ç‚º AND(ISNEW(), ISBLANK(Lead.Owner:User.Id))ã€‚é€™å€‹è¦å‰‡çš„é‚è¼¯æ˜¯ï¼šç•¶ (AND) é€™æ˜¯ä¸€ç­† æ–°å»ºç«‹çš„ (ISNEW()) è¨˜éŒ„ï¼Œè€Œä¸” (&&) é€™ç­†è¨˜éŒ„çš„ è² è²¬äººä¸æ˜¯ä¸€ä½ä½¿ç”¨è€… (ISBLANK(Lead.Owner:User.Id)) æ™‚ï¼Œé©—è­‰å¤±æ•—ï¼Œå¾è€Œé˜»æ­¢è¨˜éŒ„è¢«å„²å­˜ã€‚é€™ç¢ºä¿äº†æ–°çš„æ½›åœ¨å®¢æˆ¶åœ¨æˆç‚ºè¡ŒéŠ·æ´»å‹•æˆå“¡æ™‚ï¼Œå…¶è² è²¬äººå¿…é ˆæ˜¯ä¸€ä½å…·é«”çš„ä½¿ç”¨è€… (éŠ·å”®äººå“¡)ï¼Œè€Œä¸æ˜¯ä¸€å€‹ä½‡åˆ—ã€‚

On the gift card object, what type of field should be created to support this requirement?


Cloud Kicks (CK) æƒ³è¦è¨­å®šä¸€å€‹è‡ªè¨‚çš„å­ç‰©ä»¶ä¾†è¿½è¹¤ç™¼çµ¦å®¢æˆ¶çš„ç¦®å“å¡ã€‚ä¸€å€‹é—œéµéœ€æ±‚æ˜¯ï¼Œåœ¨ã€Œå¸³æˆ¶ (Account)ã€ä¸Šè¨˜éŒ„å·²é–‹å¡å’Œå·²ç™¼è¡Œç¦®å“å¡çš„ç¸½æ•¸ã€‚CK å¸Œæœ›æ°¸ä¹…ç¢ºä¿ç¦®å“å¡ä¸€æ—¦å»ºç«‹ï¼Œå°±ä¸èƒ½è¢«ç§»åˆ°ä»»ä½•å…¶ä»–å¸³æˆ¶ä¸‹ã€‚åœ¨ç¦®å“å¡ç‰©ä»¶ä¸Šï¼Œæ‡‰è©²å»ºç«‹å“ªç¨®é¡å‹çš„æ¬„ä½ä¾†æ”¯æ´æ­¤éœ€æ±‚ï¼Ÿ

ä¸»å¾å¼é—œä¿‚

ç¸½è¨ˆ

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): A

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The app builder should create a master-detail relationship field on the gift card object. A master-detail relationship creates a parent-child relationship where the master record controls certain behaviors of the detail record. This meets the requirements: * Track the total number: This can be done by creating roll-up summary fields on the Account object. * Permanently ensure... unable to be moved: In a master-detail relationship, the child record (gift card) cannot be "re-parented" to another master record (Account) once it is created.

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The setting for the visibility of custom tabs is default off for all users when they are deployed via change sets without including the profile settings or permission sets. When a sales rep submits an account for approval, Universal Containers wants the user to answer additional questions via a popup window to populate additional record fields. What should an app builder use to achieve the desired result?


ç•¶éŠ·å”®ä»£è¡¨æäº¤ä¸€å€‹å¸³æˆ¶ä»¥ä¾›å¯©æ ¸æ™‚ï¼ŒUniversal Containers å…¬å¸å¸Œæœ›ä½¿ç”¨è€…èƒ½é€éä¸€å€‹å½ˆå‡ºè¦–çª—å›ç­”é¡å¤–çš„å•é¡Œï¼Œä»¥å¡«å…¥è©²è¨˜éŒ„çš„å…¶ä»–æ¬„ä½ã€‚ æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æ‡‰è©²ä½¿ç”¨ä»€éº¼ä¾†é”åˆ°é æœŸçš„çµæœï¼Ÿ


A. Process Builder and Flow
Â Â Â Â Â 

Process Builder å’Œ Flow

B. Lightning component and Process Builder
Â Â Â Â Â 

Lightning å…ƒä»¶å’Œ Process Builder

C. Custom picklist field and Process Builder
Â Â Â Â Â 

è‡ªè¨‚é¸é …æ¸…å–®æ¬„ä½å’Œ Process Builder

Â Â Â Â Â 

è‡ªè¨‚æŒ‰éˆ•å’Œ Flow

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): D

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The app builder should use a custom button and Flow to achieve the desired result. A custom button is a button that can invoke custom logic or actions when clicked by a user. A Flow is a type of automation tool that can guide users through a series of screens and perform actions based on user input. In this case, the app builder can create a custom button on the Account object that launches a Flow when clicked. The Flow can display a popup window with questions for the user to answer and populate additional fields on the Account record based on the user input.
æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æ‡‰ä½¿ç”¨ã€Œè‡ªè¨‚æŒ‰éˆ•ã€å’Œã€ŒFlowã€ä¾†å¯¦ç¾æ­¤éœ€æ±‚ã€‚ä½¿ç”¨è€…é»æ“Šã€Œè‡ªè¨‚æŒ‰éˆ•ã€å¾Œå¯ä»¥è§¸ç™¼è‡ªè¨‚çš„é‚è¼¯æˆ–å‹•ä½œã€‚è€Œã€ŒFlowã€æ˜¯ä¸€ç¨®è‡ªå‹•åŒ–å·¥å…·ï¼Œå¯ä»¥å¼•å°ä½¿ç”¨è€…å®Œæˆä¸€ç³»åˆ—ç•«é¢ (screens) ä¸¦æ ¹æ“šä½¿ç”¨è€…çš„è¼¸å…¥åŸ·è¡Œæ“ä½œã€‚åœ¨æ­¤æƒ…å¢ƒä¸‹ï¼Œå»ºæ§‹è€…å¯ä»¥å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹è‡ªè¨‚æŒ‰éˆ•ä¾†å•Ÿå‹•ä¸€å€‹ Flowï¼Œé€™å€‹ Flow æœƒé¡¯ç¤ºä¸€å€‹åŒ…å«å•é¡Œçš„å½ˆå‡ºè¦–çª—ï¼Œä¸¦æ ¹æ“šä½¿ç”¨è€…çš„å›ç­”ä¾†å¡«å…¥å¸³æˆ¶è¨˜éŒ„ä¸Šçš„é¡å¤–æ¬„ä½ã€‚

ã€ç¬¬åä¸‰é¡Œ / NO. 13ã€‘


The marketing team at UVC has a list of 400 leads it wants to upload to Salesforce. The team need to avoid creating duplicate records. Which two actions should be taken to meet this requirement? (Choose 2 answers)


UVC çš„è¡ŒéŠ·åœ˜éšŠæœ‰ä¸€ä»½åŒ…å« 400 ç­†æ½›åœ¨å®¢æˆ¶çš„æ¸…å–®æƒ³è¦ä¸Šå‚³åˆ° Salesforceã€‚åœ˜éšŠéœ€è¦é¿å…å»ºç«‹é‡è¤‡çš„è¨˜éŒ„ã€‚æ‡‰æ¡å–å“ªå…©å€‹æªæ–½ä¾†æ»¿è¶³æ­¤éœ€æ±‚ï¼Ÿ(é¸æ“‡ 2 å€‹ç­”æ¡ˆ)


A. Utilize a Lead Matching Rule and corresponding Duplicate Rule to block newly created duplicate leads.
Â Â Â Â Â 

åˆ©ç”¨ã€Œæ½›åœ¨å®¢æˆ¶æ¯”å°è¦å‰‡ã€å’Œç›¸æ‡‰çš„ã€Œé‡è¤‡è¦å‰‡ã€ä¾†é˜»æ­¢æ–°å»ºç«‹çš„é‡è¤‡æ½›åœ¨å®¢æˆ¶ã€‚

B. Upload the lead list using the import wizard and select a Matching type to prevent duplicate lead creation.
Â Â Â Â Â 

ä½¿ç”¨ã€ŒåŒ¯å…¥ç²¾éˆã€ä¸Šå‚³æ½›åœ¨å®¢æˆ¶æ¸…å–®ï¼Œä¸¦é¸æ“‡ä¸€å€‹ã€Œæ¯”å°é¡å‹ã€ä»¥é˜²æ­¢å»ºç«‹é‡è¤‡çš„æ½›åœ¨å®¢æˆ¶ã€‚

C. Use Data Loader's update function to import lead and match to existing records based on e-mail address.
Â Â Â Â Â 

ä½¿ç”¨ Data Loader çš„æ›´æ–°åŠŸèƒ½åŒ¯å…¥æ½›åœ¨å®¢æˆ¶ï¼Œä¸¦æ ¹æ“šé›»å­éƒµä»¶åœ°å€èˆ‡ç¾æœ‰è¨˜éŒ„é€²è¡Œæ¯”å°ã€‚

D. Enable Duplicate Matching in the Data Management section in Setup and activate the Lead-to_Lead scenario.
Â Â Â Â Â 

åœ¨ã€Œè¨­å®šã€çš„ã€Œè³‡æ–™ç®¡ç†ã€éƒ¨åˆ†å•Ÿç”¨ã€Œé‡è¤‡æ¯”å°ã€ï¼Œä¸¦å•Ÿå‹•ã€Œæ½›åœ¨å®¢æˆ¶å°æ½›åœ¨å®¢æˆ¶ã€çš„æƒ…å¢ƒã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): A, B

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The best actions to take to avoid creating duplicate leads when uploading a list of 400 leads are to utilize a Lead Matching Rule and corresponding Duplicate Rule to block newly created duplicate leads, and to upload the lead list using the import wizard and select a Matching type to prevent duplicate lead creation. The Lead Matching Rule defines the criteria for identifying duplicate leads, and the Duplicate Rule defines the actions to take when a duplicate is detected. The import wizard allows users to choose a Matching type based on the Lead Matching Rule and block or allow duplicates.

The best way to configure Account sharing so that community users only see their own Account is to set the account external OWD to private. This will restrict the access to Account records for external users.

é¸æ“‡æ­£ç¢ºçš„è¨˜éŒ„é¡å‹ã€‚

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): C, D

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The two steps that should be suggested are to select insert null values in settings and to use Data Loader to update leads using the CSV file. Selecting insert null values in settings will allow Data Loader to overwrite existing values with null values. Data Loader is a tool that can import, export, update, or delete large amounts of data. (Note: Import Wizard has a limit of 50,000 records, but Data Loader is generally preferred for this type of mass update operation).

è®Šæ›´é›†ä¸åŒ…å«æ‰€æœ‰å…ƒä»¶ï¼Œå¯èƒ½éœ€è¦æ‰‹å‹•åŸ·è¡Œä¸€äº›è®Šæ›´ã€‚

åœ¨æ¥æ”¶å‚³å…¥çš„è®Šæ›´é›†æ™‚ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨è€…æ‡‰è©²ç™»å‡ºç”Ÿç”¢ç’°å¢ƒã€‚

å¦‚æœéƒ¨ç½²å‡ºéŒ¯ï¼Œäº¤æ˜“å°‡æœƒé‚„åŸã€‚

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): B, C (è¨»ï¼šæ ¹æ“šé¡Œåº«æ–‡ä»¶æä¾›çš„ç­”æ¡ˆã€‚åœ¨å¯¦å‹™ä¸Š D ä¹Ÿæ˜¯ä¸€å€‹æ­£ç¢ºçš„è€ƒé‡ï¼Œå› ç‚º Salesforce éƒ¨ç½²æ˜¯äº¤æ˜“å¼çš„ï¼Œå¤±æ•—æœƒè‡ªå‹•å›å¾©ã€‚ä½† C ä½œç‚ºæœ€ä½³å¯¦è¸ï¼Œæ˜¯ç‚ºäº†é¿å…éƒ¨ç½²éç¨‹ä¸­ç™¼ç”Ÿè¡çªã€‚)

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The two considerations that an app builder should keep in mind are: Change sets do not include all components and may have to perform some changes manually. Change sets do not support all types of components, such as reports, dashboards, email templates, etc. Users should be logged out of production when receiving inbound change sets. This is a best practice to avoid any errors or conflicts that may occur when deploying changes to production.

Cloud Kicks has five years of sales data and would like to track when customers made their first purchase.
How should an app builder use a roll-up summary to meet the requirements?


Cloud Kicks å…¬å¸æ“æœ‰äº”å¹´çš„éŠ·å”®è³‡æ–™ï¼Œä¸¦å¸Œæœ›è¿½è¹¤å®¢æˆ¶é¦–æ¬¡è³¼è²·çš„æ™‚é–“ã€‚
æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æ‡‰å¦‚ä½•ä½¿ç”¨ç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½ä¾†æ»¿è¶³æ­¤éœ€æ±‚ï¼Ÿ


A. Create a new roll-up summary field called First Order Date, using Type MIN on the Opportunity Close Date with a filter where IsWon = TRU

E.
Â Â Â Â Â 

å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹åç‚ºã€Œé¦–æ¬¡è¨‚å–®æ—¥æœŸã€çš„ç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½ï¼Œå°ã€Œæ©ŸæœƒçµæŸæ—¥æœŸã€ä½¿ç”¨ MIN (æœ€å°å€¼) é¡å‹ï¼Œä¸¦è¨­å®šç¯©é¸æ¢ä»¶ç‚º IsWon = TRUEã€‚

E.
Â Â Â Â Â 

å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹åç‚ºã€Œé¦–æ¬¡è¨‚å–®æ—¥æœŸã€çš„æ—¥æœŸæ¬„ä½ï¼Œå»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹æ–°çš„å·¥ä½œæµç¨‹ä¾†è¨­å®šæ—¥æœŸï¼Œä¸¦ä½¿ç”¨ç¯©é¸æ¢ä»¶ IsWon = TRUE ä¾†åŒ¯ç¸½è©²å€¼ã€‚

C. Create a new roll-up summary field called First Order Date, using Type SUM on Opportunity Close Date.
Â Â Â Â Â 

å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹åç‚ºã€Œé¦–æ¬¡è¨‚å–®æ—¥æœŸã€çš„ç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½ï¼Œå°ã€Œæ©ŸæœƒçµæŸæ—¥æœŸã€ä½¿ç”¨ SUM (åŠ ç¸½) é¡å‹ã€‚

Â Â Â Â Â 

å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹åç‚ºã€Œé¦–æ¬¡è¨‚å–®æ—¥æœŸã€çš„æ—¥æœŸæ¬„ä½ï¼Œç„¶å¾Œå»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹ç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨ MIN (æœ€å°å€¼) é¡å‹ä¾†æ›´æ–°è©²æ¬„ä½ã€‚

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): A

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The app builder should create a new roll-up summary field called First Order Date, using Type MIN on the Opportunity Close Date with a filter where IsWon = TRU

E. A roll-up summary field calculates values from related records. In this case, the app builder can create a roll-up summary field on the Account object that calculates the minimum (earliest) value of the Opportunity Close Date field from the related opportunities where IsWon = TRU

E. This will show when customers made their first purchase.

An app builder has downloaded a component from the AppExchange successfully; however, they are unable to add it to the Lightning home page.

A. My Domain must be deployed to add custom components to the page with the App Builder.
Â Â Â Â Â 

å¿…é ˆéƒ¨ç½²ã€Œæˆ‘çš„ç¶²åŸŸ (My Domain)ã€ï¼Œæ‰èƒ½ä½¿ç”¨ App Builder å°‡è‡ªè¨‚å…ƒä»¶æ–°å¢åˆ°é é¢ã€‚

Â Â Â Â Â 

å¿…é ˆå»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹è‡ªè¨‚ç´¢å¼•æ¨™ç±¤ï¼Œæ‰èƒ½ä½¿ç”¨ App Builder å°‡è‡ªè¨‚å…ƒä»¶æ–°å¢åˆ°é é¢ã€‚

è©²å…ƒä»¶éœ€è¦é–‹ç™¼äººå“¡æ¬Šé™æ‰èƒ½ä½¿ç”¨ App Builder å°‡å…¶æ–°å¢åˆ°é é¢ã€‚

D. The component is tagged for record pages instead of home pages and is not showing up in the App Builder.
Â Â Â Â Â 

è©²å…ƒä»¶è¢«æ¨™è¨˜ç‚ºç”¨æ–¼ã€Œè¨˜éŒ„é é¢ã€è€Œéã€Œé¦–é ã€ï¼Œå› æ­¤æœªé¡¯ç¤ºåœ¨ App Builder ä¸­ã€‚

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): A, D

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
Two reasons that can prevent an app builder from adding a custom component to the Lightning home page are if My Domain is not deployed, or if the component is tagged for record pages instead of home pages. My Domain must be deployed to add custom components to the page with the App Builder, as it enables Lightning components and other features. The component must be tagged for home pages in its configuration file, otherwise it will not show up in the App Builder for home pages.

DreamHouse Realty is rethinking its sandbox utilization strategy after acquiring Cloud Kicks. The Salesforce COE already utilizes a partial and a full sandbox, which it refreshes on their own regular schedules. Teams are expanding and have to begin each of their small projects in a sandbox before committing to the larger pool for collaborative testing while still keeping costs down.
What type of sandbox should each team member use?


åœ¨æ”¶è³¼ Cloud Kicks ä¹‹å¾Œï¼ŒDreamHouse Realty æ­£åœ¨é‡æ–°æ€è€ƒå…¶æ²™ç®±ä½¿ç”¨ç­–ç•¥ã€‚Salesforce å“è¶Šä¸­å¿ƒ (COE) å·²ç¶“åœ¨ä½¿ç”¨ä¸€å€‹ Partial Sandbox å’Œä¸€å€‹ Full Sandboxï¼Œä¸¦æŒ‰å„è‡ªçš„å¸¸è¦æ™‚é–“è¡¨é€²è¡Œé‡æ–°æ•´ç†ã€‚ç¾åœ¨åœ˜éšŠæ­£åœ¨æ“´å¤§ï¼Œæ¯å€‹å°å‹å°ˆæ¡ˆéƒ½å¿…é ˆåœ¨ä¸€å€‹æ²™ç®±ä¸­é–‹å§‹ï¼Œç„¶å¾Œå†æäº¤åˆ°æ›´å¤§çš„æ± ä¸­é€²è¡Œå”åŒæ¸¬è©¦ï¼ŒåŒæ™‚é‚„è¦æ§åˆ¶æˆæœ¬ã€‚
æ¯å€‹åœ˜éšŠæˆå“¡æ‡‰è©²ä½¿ç”¨å“ªç¨®é¡å‹çš„æ²™ç®±ï¼Ÿ


A. Full sandbox
Â Â Â Â Â 

å®Œæ•´æ²™ç®±

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): B

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The best type of sandbox for each team member to use is a developer sandbox. A developer sandbox is a copy of production that includes only the metadata. It does not include any data. A developer sandbox is ideal for small projects that do not require data testing, such as developing new features or customizations. A developer sandbox is also cheaper than other types of sandboxes.

ã€ç¬¬ä¸‰åä¸ƒé¡Œ / NO. 37ã€‘


Universal Containers uses a private sharing model on Accounts. User A and user B both own Accounts of their own and have both been sent a new account record in an email owned by user C to take a look at. User A is able to open and view the record but user B receives an insufficient privileges error. User A and user B have the same role in the role hierarchy as user C .
What are the three reasons user A has access but user B is unable to access the record? (Choose 3 answers)


Universal Containers å…¬å¸çš„ã€Œå¸³æˆ¶ã€æ¡ç”¨ç§äººå…±ç”¨æ¨¡å‹ã€‚ä½¿ç”¨è€… A å’Œä½¿ç”¨è€… B å„è‡ªæ“æœ‰è‡ªå·±çš„å¸³æˆ¶ï¼Œä»–å€‘éƒ½æ”¶åˆ°ä¸€å°ç”±ä½¿ç”¨è€… C æ“æœ‰çš„æ–°å¸³æˆ¶è¨˜éŒ„çš„é›»å­éƒµä»¶ï¼Œè®“ä»–å€‘æŸ¥çœ‹ã€‚ä½¿ç”¨è€… A èƒ½å¤ æ‰“é–‹ä¸¦æª¢è¦–è©²è¨˜éŒ„ï¼Œä½†ä½¿ç”¨è€… B å»æ”¶åˆ°æ¬Šé™ä¸è¶³çš„éŒ¯èª¤ã€‚ä½¿ç”¨è€… Aã€B å’Œ C åœ¨è§’è‰²å±¤ç´šçµæ§‹ä¸­æ“”ä»»ç›¸åŒçš„è§’è‰²ã€‚
ä½¿ç”¨è€… A æœ‰å­˜å–æ¬Šé™è€Œä½¿ç”¨è€… B æ²’æœ‰çš„ä¸‰å€‹å¯èƒ½åŸå› æ˜¯ä»€éº¼ï¼Ÿ(é¸æ“‡ 3 å€‹ç­”æ¡ˆ)


A. User A is on the same account team as user C .
Â Â Â Â Â 

ä½¿ç”¨è€… A å’Œä½¿ç”¨è€… C åœ¨åŒä¸€å€‹å¸³æˆ¶åœ˜éšŠä¸­ã€‚

B. User A and user B have different profiles.
Â Â Â Â Â 

ä½¿ç”¨è€… A å’Œä½¿ç”¨è€… B æœ‰ä¸åŒçš„è¨­å®šæª”ã€‚

C. User C has manually shared the record with user A .
Â Â Â Â Â 

ä½¿ç”¨è€… C æ‰‹å‹•å°‡è©²è¨˜éŒ„èˆ‡ä½¿ç”¨è€… A å…±ç”¨ã€‚

D. User A was granted an additional permission set.
Â Â Â Â Â 

ä½¿ç”¨è€… A è¢«æˆäºˆäº†ä¸€å€‹é¡å¤–çš„æ¬Šé™é›†ã€‚

E. User A is in a public group that has access via a sharing rule.
Â Â Â Â Â 

ä½¿ç”¨è€… A æ‰€åœ¨çš„ä¸€å€‹å…¬é–‹ç¾¤çµ„é€éå…±ç”¨è¦å‰‡ç²å¾—äº†å­˜å–æ¬Šé™ã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): A, C, E

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The three reasons user A has access but user B is unable to access the record are: 1. User A is on the same account team as user C . 2. User C has manually shared the record with user A . 3. User A is in a public group that has access via a sharing rule. All these are record-level sharing mechanisms that can grant access beyond the role hierarchy. Different profiles (B) or permission sets (D) grant object-level permissions, not specific record access in a private model.

ç”±æ–¼ Universal Containers æ²™ç®±ç™¼å¸ƒæ’ç¨‹å’Œéœ€æ±‚çš„è¤‡é›œæ€§ï¼Œå»ºè­°ç›¡å¯èƒ½é »ç¹åœ°ä½¿ç”¨è®Šæ›´é›†å°‡è®Šæ›´å¾ä¸€å€‹ç’°å¢ƒé·ç§»åˆ°å¦ä¸€å€‹ç’°å¢ƒã€‚

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): C, D, E

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The common items that can be moved using a change set are custom object, Apex class, and custom field. These are metadata components that can be deployed from one environment to another using change sets. Web-to-lead settings and standard fields are not metadata components that can be moved using change sets.

Universal Containers å…¬å¸ä½¿ç”¨ã€Œè³‡ç”¢ (Asset)ã€ç‰©ä»¶ä¾†è¿½è¹¤å®‰è£åœ¨å®¢æˆ¶åœ°é»çš„ç”¢å“ã€‚ç¾åœ¨å»ºç«‹äº†ä¸€å€‹æ–°ç‰©ä»¶ã€Œè³‡ç”¢åº«å­˜ (Asset Inventory)ã€ï¼Œç”¨ä¾†æ“·å–é—œæ–¼è³‡ç”¢çš„è©³ç´°è³‡è¨Šã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): A, C

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
Workflow rule and an outbound message or Process Builder and Apex Code are two ways to integrate Salesforce with an external web service. Workflow rule can define criteria and actions for triggering an outbound message, which is an XML message sent to a designated endpoint URL. Process Builder can invoke Apex Code, which is a programming language that can make callouts to external web services using HTTP requests. (Note: Process Builder can also trigger an outbound message, making option D also viable in practice. However, the provided answer is A and C).

Ursa Major Solar's service department gets requests for several types of services, such as installation, repair, and maintenance. Service managers need to be able to tell when maintenance was last done on on asset to help determine if they are meeting contract agreements, but the last maintenance date can be difficult to determine when there are many work orders related to the asset. They think it would be helpful to have a field auto-populated on the Asset record when a maintenance work order gets closed.
What tool should an app builder recommend to help meet this requirement?


Ursa Major Solar çš„æœå‹™éƒ¨é–€æœƒæ”¶åˆ°å¤šç¨®é¡å‹çš„æœå‹™è«‹æ±‚ï¼Œå¦‚å®‰è£ã€ç¶­ä¿®å’Œä¿é¤Šã€‚æœå‹™ç¶“ç†éœ€è¦èƒ½å¤ çŸ¥é“è³‡ç”¢ä¸Šæ¬¡é€²è¡Œä¿é¤Šçš„æ™‚é–“ï¼Œä»¥å¹«åŠ©åˆ¤æ–·æ˜¯å¦ç¬¦åˆåˆç´„å”è­°ï¼Œä½†ç•¶è³‡ç”¢æœ‰è¨±å¤šç›¸é—œå·¥å–®æ™‚ï¼Œå¾ˆé›£ç¢ºå®šä¸Šæ¬¡ä¿é¤Šæ—¥æœŸã€‚ä»–å€‘èªç‚ºï¼Œå¦‚æœç•¶ä¿é¤Šå·¥å–®çµæ¡ˆæ™‚ï¼Œèƒ½è‡ªå‹•åœ¨è³‡ç”¢è¨˜éŒ„ä¸Šå¡«å…¥ä¸€å€‹æ¬„ä½ï¼Œå°‡æœƒå¾ˆæœ‰å¹«åŠ©ã€‚
æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æ‡‰æ¨è–¦ä½¿ç”¨å“ªç¨®å·¥å…·ä¾†æ»¿è¶³æ­¤éœ€æ±‚ï¼Ÿ

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): D

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
A flow is an application that automates a business process. You can use flows to update fields on related records when a certain event occurs, such as closing a work order. In this case, a flow can be used to update the last maintenance date field on the Asset record when a maintenance work order gets closed. (Note: A roll-up summary can only work with a Master-Detail relationship, which may not exist between Asset and Work Order).

Flow æ˜¯ä¸€å€‹å¯ä»¥è‡ªå‹•åŒ–æ¥­å‹™æµç¨‹çš„æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼ã€‚æ‚¨å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨ Flow åœ¨ç‰¹å®šäº‹ä»¶ç™¼ç”Ÿæ™‚ï¼ˆä¾‹å¦‚å·¥å–®çµæ¡ˆï¼‰æ›´æ–°ç›¸é—œè¨˜éŒ„ä¸Šçš„æ¬„ä½ã€‚åœ¨é€™å€‹æƒ…å¢ƒä¸­ï¼Œå¯ä»¥å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹ç”±ã€Œå·¥å–®ã€è¨˜éŒ„è§¸ç™¼çš„ Flowï¼Œç•¶å·¥å–®ç‹€æ…‹è®Šç‚ºã€Œå·²çµæ¡ˆã€ä¸”é¡å‹ç‚ºã€Œä¿é¤Šã€æ™‚ï¼ŒFlow æœƒè‡ªå‹•å°‡è©²å·¥å–®çš„çµæ¡ˆæ—¥æœŸæ›´æ–°åˆ°ç›¸é—œã€Œè³‡ç”¢ã€è¨˜éŒ„çš„ã€Œä¸Šæ¬¡ä¿é¤Šæ—¥æœŸã€æ¬„ä½ä¸­ã€‚ (è¨»ï¼šç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½éœ€è¦ä¸»å¾å¼é—œä¿‚ï¼Œè€Œè³‡ç”¢å’Œå·¥å–®ä¹‹é–“é€šå¸¸ä¸æ˜¯ä¸»å¾å¼é—œä¿‚ï¼Œå› æ­¤ä¸é©ç”¨)ã€‚

At Universal Containers, the Account object has a Master-Detail relationship with an Invoice custom object. The App Builder would like to change to a lookup field, but is not able to do so.
What could be causing this?


åœ¨ Universal Containersï¼Œå¸³æˆ¶ç‰©ä»¶èˆ‡ä¸€å€‹è‡ªè¨‚çš„ç™¼ç¥¨ç‰©ä»¶ä¹‹é–“å­˜åœ¨ä¸»å¾å¼é—œä¿‚ã€‚æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æƒ³è¦å°‡å…¶æ›´æ”¹ç‚ºæŸ¥è©¢æ¬„ä½ï¼Œä½†ç„¡æ³•é€™éº¼åšã€‚
å¯èƒ½çš„åŸå› æ˜¯ä»€éº¼ï¼Ÿ


A. The invoice must have at least one Master-Detail field for reporting.
Â Â Â Â Â 

ç™¼ç¥¨ç‰©ä»¶å¿…é ˆè‡³å°‘æœ‰ä¸€å€‹ä¸»å¾å¼æ¬„ä½ç”¨æ–¼å ±å‘Šã€‚

B. The Account record includes Invoice roll-up summary fields.
Â Â Â Â Â 

å¸³æˆ¶è¨˜éŒ„ä¸ŠåŒ…å«äº†ç™¼ç¥¨çš„ç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½ã€‚

C. The Invoice records have existing values in the Account.
Â Â Â Â Â 

ç™¼ç¥¨è¨˜éŒ„åœ¨å¸³æˆ¶æ¬„ä½ä¸­å·²å­˜åœ¨å€¼ã€‚

D. The Account is included in the workflow on the Invoice object.
Â Â Â Â Â 

å¸³æˆ¶è¢«åŒ…å«åœ¨ç™¼ç¥¨ç‰©ä»¶çš„å·¥ä½œæµç¨‹ä¸­ã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): B

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The Account record includes Invoice roll-up summary fields. This is correct because roll-up summary fields are only available on the master object in a master-detail relationship, and changing the field type to lookup would delete the roll-up summary fields. You must delete the roll-up summary fields before you can convert the relationship type.

æ­£ç¢ºç­”æ¡ˆæ˜¯å¸³æˆ¶è¨˜éŒ„ä¸ŠåŒ…å«äº†ç™¼ç¥¨çš„ç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½ã€‚ç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½ (roll-up summary fields) æ˜¯ä¸»å¾å¼é—œä¿‚ç¨æœ‰çš„åŠŸèƒ½ï¼Œå®ƒå€‘åªèƒ½å­˜åœ¨æ–¼ä¸»ç‰©ä»¶ä¸Šã€‚å¦‚æœè¦å°‡ä¸»å¾å¼é—œä¿‚è½‰æ›ç‚ºæŸ¥è©¢é—œä¿‚ï¼Œå¿…é ˆå…ˆæ‰‹å‹•åˆªé™¤ä¸»ç‰©ä»¶ä¸Šæ‰€æœ‰å¼•ç”¨è©²å¾ç‰©ä»¶çš„ç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½ã€‚

ã€ç¬¬å››åå…­é¡Œ / NO. 46ã€‘


At Universal Containers, the VP of Service has requested a visual indicator flag on each case, based on the case priority. High-priority cases should be flagged red, medium-priority should be flagged yellow, and low-priority cases should be flagged green.
Which formula would accomplish this requirement? (Choose 2 answers)


Universal Containers çš„æœå‹™å‰¯ç¸½è¦æ±‚åœ¨æ¯å€‹å€‹æ¡ˆä¸Šæ ¹æ“šå…¶å„ªå…ˆé †åºé¡¯ç¤ºä¸€å€‹è¦–è¦ºæŒ‡ç¤ºæ——å¹Ÿã€‚é«˜å„ªå…ˆé †åºçš„å€‹æ¡ˆæ‡‰æ¨™è¨˜ç‚ºç´…è‰²ï¼Œä¸­å„ªå…ˆé †åºç‚ºé»ƒè‰²ï¼Œä½å„ªå…ˆé †åºç‚ºç¶ è‰²ã€‚
å“ªå€‹å…¬å¼å¯ä»¥å®Œæˆæ­¤éœ€æ±‚ï¼Ÿ(é¸æ“‡ 2 å€‹ç­”æ¡ˆ)
(è¨»ï¼šé¸é …ä¸­åœ–ç‰‡è·¯å¾‘ç‚ºç¯„ä¾‹)


A. CASE (Priority, "Low", "img/samples/flag_green.gif", "Medium", "img/samples/flag_yellow.gif", "High", "img/samples/flag_red.gif", "/s.gif")

B. IMAGE (IF(ISPICKVAL (Priority, "Low"), "img/samples/flag_green.gif", IF (ISPICKVAL (Priority, "Medium"), "img/samples/flag_yellow.gif", IF(ISPICKVAL (Priority, "High"), "img/samples/flag_red.gif"))), "Priority Flag")

C. IF (ISPICKVAL(Priority, "Low"), "img/samples/flag_green.gif", IF (ISPICKVAL (Priority, "Medium"), "img/samples/flag_yellow.gif", IF (ISPICKVAL (Priority, "High"), "img/samples/flag_red.gif", "/s.gif"))

D. IMAGE (CASE(Priority, "Low", "img/samples/flag_green.gif", "Medium", "img/samples/flag_yellow.gif", "High", "img/samples/flag_red.gif", "Priority Flag")
(è¨»ï¼šé¸é …Dçš„å…¬å¼ç¼ºå°‘äº†æœ€å¾Œä¸€å€‹ else_result åƒæ•¸ï¼Œèªæ³•ä¸å®Œæ•´)


é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): A, D (æ ¹æ“šé¡Œåº«ï¼Œå„˜ç®¡ D èªæ³•æœ‰èª¤)

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The formula for creating a visual indicator flag on each case based on the case priority should use the IMAGE and CASE functions. The IMAGE function returns an image for a given URL, and the CASE function evaluates an expression and returns a value based on that expression. Option A and D use these functions correctly, while option B and C do not. (Note: Option A is missing the IMAGE() wrapper to actually display the image, and Option D is missing a parameter in the CASE function. However, the logic of using CASE is correct. The most complete answer is B, but we follow the provided answer key).

ç‚ºäº†é¡¯ç¤ºåœ–ç‰‡ï¼Œå¿…é ˆä½¿ç”¨ IMAGE() å‡½æ•¸ã€‚ç‚ºäº†æ ¹æ“šé¸é …æ¸…å–® (picklist) çš„å€¼ä¾†é¸æ“‡ä¸åŒçš„åœ–ç‰‡è·¯å¾‘ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨ CASE() å‡½æ•¸æ¯”å·¢ç‹€çš„ IF() å‡½æ•¸æ›´ç°¡æ½”ã€‚
é¸é … Aï¼šä½¿ç”¨äº† CASE å‡½æ•¸ä¾†è¿”å›åœ–ç‰‡è·¯å¾‘ï¼Œä½†ç¼ºå°‘äº†å¤–å±¤çš„ IMAGE() å‡½æ•¸ä¾†å°‡è·¯å¾‘è½‰æ›ç‚ºåœ–ç‰‡ã€‚
é¸é … Bï¼šä½¿ç”¨äº† IMAGE() å’Œå·¢ç‹€çš„ IF()ï¼Œèªæ³•å’Œé‚è¼¯å®Œå…¨æ­£ç¢ºã€‚
é¸é … Cï¼šä½¿ç”¨äº†å·¢ç‹€çš„ IF()ï¼Œä½†ç¼ºå°‘äº†å¤–å±¤çš„ IMAGE() å‡½æ•¸ã€‚
é¸é … Dï¼šä½¿ç”¨äº† IMAGE() å’Œ CASE()ï¼Œä½† CASE å‡½æ•¸çš„èªæ³•ä¸å®Œæ•´ï¼Œç¼ºå°‘äº†æœ€å¾Œä¸€å€‹ã€Œå…¶ä»–æƒ…æ³ (else_result)ã€çš„åƒæ•¸ã€‚
å„˜ç®¡é¸é … B æ˜¯èªæ³•æœ€å®Œæ•´çš„ï¼Œä½†é¡Œåº«ç­”æ¡ˆç‚º A å’Œ Dï¼Œå¯èƒ½æ˜¯å› ç‚ºå®ƒå€‘å±•ç¤ºäº† CASE å‡½æ•¸çš„ç”¨æ³•ã€‚ä¸€å€‹å®Œå…¨æ­£ç¢ºçš„å¯«æ³•æ‡‰è©²æ˜¯ï¼š

To insert a list of 25,000 records using deduplication for the Race_Track__c custom object, an app builder should use Data Loader. Cloud Kicks wants to make sure that users without the Marketing role are unable to update the Contact Retail_Opt_In__c picklist field to Yes.
What validation rule would an app builder use to prevent other users from making this update?


Cloud Kicks å¸Œæœ›ç¢ºä¿æ²’æœ‰ã€Œè¡ŒéŠ· (Marketing)ã€è§’è‰²çš„ä½¿ç”¨è€…ç„¡æ³•å°‡é€£çµ¡äººçš„ Retail_Opt_In__c é¸é …æ¸…å–®æ¬„ä½æ›´æ–°ç‚ºã€Œæ˜¯ (Yes)ã€ã€‚
æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æ‡‰è©²ä½¿ç”¨å“ªæ¢é©—è­‰è¦å‰‡ä¾†é˜»æ­¢å…¶ä»–ä½¿ç”¨è€…é€²è¡Œæ­¤æ›´æ–°ï¼Ÿ


A. AND($UserRole.Name != 'Marketing', ISCHANGED(Retail_Opt_In__c), ISPICKVAL(Retail_Opt_In__c, "Yes"))

B. AND($UserRole.Name != 'Marketing', Retail_Opt_In__c = "Yes")

C. AND($UserRole.Name = 'Marketing', ISPICKVAL(Retail_Opt_In__c, "Yes"))

D. AND($UserRole.Name = 'Marketing', Retail_Opt_In__c = "Yes")


é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): A

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The validation rule should check if the user role is not Marketing, and if the Retail_Opt_In__c field has been changed to Yes. The ISCHANGED function returns true if the field value has been changed, and the ISPICKVAL function returns true if the field value matches a specified picklist value.

An App Builder wants to deploy a new version of an auto launched flow to production in an active state so that the new functionality Is immediately available to users. What should the App Builder take into consideration when planning the deployment?


ä¸€ä½æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æƒ³è¦éƒ¨ç½²ä¸€å€‹æ–°ç‰ˆæœ¬çš„è‡ªå‹•å•Ÿå‹•æµç¨‹ (auto-launched flow) åˆ°ç”Ÿç”¢ç’°å¢ƒï¼Œä¸¦ä½¿å…¶è™•æ–¼å•Ÿç”¨ç‹€æ…‹ï¼Œä»¥ä¾¿æ–°åŠŸèƒ½èƒ½ç«‹å³å°ä½¿ç”¨è€…å¯ç”¨ã€‚åœ¨è¦åŠƒéƒ¨ç½²æ™‚ï¼Œå»ºæ§‹è€…æ‡‰è€ƒæ…®ä»€éº¼ï¼Ÿ


A. Verify there is an Apex test that provides test coverage for the Flow.
Â Â Â Â Â 

é©—è­‰æ˜¯å¦æœ‰ä¸€å€‹ç‚º Flow æä¾›æ¸¬è©¦è¦†è“‹ç‡çš„ Apex æ¸¬è©¦ã€‚

B. Grant user access to the Flow.
Â Â Â Â Â 

æˆäºˆä½¿ç”¨è€…å° Flow çš„å­˜å–æ¬Šé™ã€‚

C. Manually activate the Flow after deployment
Â Â Â Â Â 

éƒ¨ç½²å¾Œæ‰‹å‹•å•Ÿå‹• Flowã€‚

D. Include the Process Builder calling the Flow In the deployment
Â Â Â Â Â 

åœ¨éƒ¨ç½²ä¸­åŒ…å«å‘¼å«è©² Flow çš„ Process Builderã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): A

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The app builder should verify that there is an Apex test that provides test coverage for the Flow. An Apex test is a unit test that verifies the functionality and quality of Apex code. Apex tests are required to deploy any change that contains Apex code or references Apex code, such as an auto launched flow. The app builder should ensure that there is an Apex test that covers at least 75% of the Flow logic before deploying it to production in an active state.

å»ºæ§‹è€…æ‡‰é©—è­‰æ˜¯å¦æœ‰ä¸€å€‹ç‚º Flow æä¾›æ¸¬è©¦è¦†è“‹ç‡çš„ Apex æ¸¬è©¦ã€‚ åœ¨éƒ¨ç½²åŒ…å« Apex ç¨‹å¼ç¢¼æˆ–è¢« Apex ç¨‹å¼ç¢¼å¼•ç”¨çš„è®Šæ›´æ™‚ï¼ŒApex æ¸¬è©¦æ˜¯å¿…éœ€çš„ã€‚ ç”±æ–¼è‡ªå‹•å•Ÿå‹•æµç¨‹å¯ä»¥è¢« Apex è§¸ç™¼ï¼ŒSalesforce åœ¨éƒ¨ç½²æ™‚æœƒå°‡å…¶è¦–ç‚ºéœ€è¦æ¸¬è©¦è¦†è“‹ç‡çš„å…ƒä»¶ï¼Œä»¥ç¢ºä¿å…¶é‚è¼¯çš„ç©©å®šæ€§ï¼Œå°¤å…¶æ˜¯ç•¶æ‚¨å¸Œæœ›å®ƒä¸€ç¶“éƒ¨ç½²å°±ç«‹å³è™•æ–¼ã€Œå•Ÿç”¨ã€ç‹€æ…‹æ™‚ã€‚

Universal Containers is expecting impacts to operations due to increased demand. The executive team will be reaching out to current customers and want to see the number of open cases for the account and parent account.

ç”±æ–¼éœ€æ±‚å¢åŠ ï¼ŒUniversal Containers é è¨ˆç‡Ÿé‹å°‡å—åˆ°å½±éŸ¿ã€‚é«˜éšä¸»ç®¡åœ˜éšŠå°‡è¯ç¹«ç¾æœ‰å®¢æˆ¶ï¼Œä¸¦å¸Œæœ›çœ‹åˆ°è©²å¸³æˆ¶åŠå…¶çˆ¶å¸³æˆ¶çš„æœªçµæ¡ˆå€‹æ¡ˆæ•¸é‡ã€‚
æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…å¯ä»¥çµåˆå“ªå…©ç¨®å·¥å…·ä¾†åœ¨å¸³æˆ¶é é¢ä¸Šé¡¯ç¤ºæœªçµæ¡ˆå€‹æ¡ˆçš„æ•¸é‡ï¼Ÿ(é¸æ“‡ 2 å€‹ç­”æ¡ˆ)

B. Workflow

å·¥ä½œæµç¨‹

Â Â Â Â Â

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The two tools that an app builder could combine to display the number of open cases on the account page are Flow and Process Builder. Flow is a tool that allows the app builder to create a declarative automation that can query, manipulate, and display data from multiple objects. Process Builder is a tool that allows the app builder to create a trigger-based automation that can invoke a Flow when a record is created or updated.

An app builder wants to create a report to compare the number of support cases in each status (New, In-progress, or Closed) and by priority (Critical, High, Medium, or Low).
What solution should be used for the report?


ä¸€ä½æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æƒ³è¦å»ºç«‹ä¸€ä»½å ±å‘Šï¼Œä»¥æ¯”è¼ƒæ¯å€‹ç‹€æ…‹ï¼ˆæ–°å¢ã€è™•ç†ä¸­æˆ–å·²çµæ¡ˆï¼‰å’Œæ¯å€‹å„ªå…ˆé †åºï¼ˆåš´é‡ã€é«˜ã€ä¸­æˆ–ä½ï¼‰çš„æ”¯æ´å€‹æ¡ˆæ•¸é‡ã€‚
æ‡‰è©²ä½¿ç”¨å“ªç¨®è§£æ±ºæ–¹æ¡ˆä¾†è£½ä½œæ­¤å ±å‘Šï¼Ÿ


A. Grouping
Â Â Â Â Â 

ç¾¤çµ„

B. Bucket Columns
Â Â Â Â Â 

åˆ†é¡æ¬„

C. Custom Report Type
Â Â Â Â Â 

è‡ªè¨‚å ±å‘Šé¡å‹

D. Filters
Â Â Â Â Â 

ç¯©é¸å™¨

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): A

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The best solution to create a report to compare the number of support cases in each status and by priority is to use grouping. Grouping allows the app builder to summarize data by one or more fields, such as status and priority, and display them in rows and columns. This requires a Summary or Matrix report format.

Â Â Â Â Â

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
To manually share individual records with specific people or group of people on a case by case basis, users can use public groups, roles, or users. The Director of customer service wants to receive a notification when a case stays in the "new" status for more than four business hours.
Which two automation processes should be used to accomplish this? (Choose 2 answers)


å®¢æˆ¶æœå‹™ç¸½ç›£å¸Œæœ›ç•¶ä¸€å€‹å€‹æ¡ˆåœ¨ã€Œæ–°å¢ã€ç‹€æ…‹ä¸‹åœç•™è¶…éå››å€‹å·¥ä½œå°æ™‚å¾Œï¼Œèƒ½æ”¶åˆ°ä¸€å‰‡é€šçŸ¥ã€‚
æ‡‰è©²ä½¿ç”¨å“ªå…©å€‹è‡ªå‹•åŒ–æµç¨‹ä¾†å®Œæˆæ­¤ä»»å‹™ï¼Ÿ(é¸æ“‡ 2 å€‹ç­”æ¡ˆ)


A. Escalation rules
Â Â Â Â Â 

å‘ˆå ±è¦å‰‡

B. Flow Builder

C. Process Builder

D. Scheduled Apex
Â Â Â Â Â 

å·²æ’ç¨‹çš„ Apex

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): A, C (è¨»ï¼šç¾åœ¨å»ºè­°ä½¿ç”¨ Flow å–ä»£ Process Builder)

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
Escalation rules and Process Builder are two automation processes that can be used to send a notification. Escalation rules can define criteria and actions for escalating cases based on time or other factors. Process Builder can create a time-based action that triggers an email alert when the case status is "new" for more than four business hours.

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
Changing custom field types may result in data loss if the new field type is incompatible with the old one. Field history tracking records value changes of 255 characters or less. If a rich text field value exceeds this limit, only the first 255 characters are tracked.

å¦‚æœæ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…å˜—è©¦å°‡ä¸€å€‹å·²æœ‰çš„é•·æ–‡å­—å€åŸŸæ¬„ä½è½‰æ›ç‚ºæ–‡å­—å€åŸŸï¼Œç¾æœ‰çš„è³‡è¨Šæœƒç™¼ç”Ÿä»€éº¼æƒ…æ³ï¼Ÿ
(è¨»ï¼šæ–‡å­—å€åŸŸ (Text Area) é è¨­é•·åº¦ç‚º 255 å­—å…ƒ)


A. Preexisting information will truncate to the first 255 characters.
Â Â Â Â Â 

å·²æœ‰çš„è³‡è¨Šå°‡è¢«æˆªæ–·ç‚ºå‰ 255 å€‹å­—å…ƒã€‚

æ¬„ä½ä¸­å·²æœ‰çš„è³‡è¨Šå°‡å®Œå…¨éºå¤±ã€‚

C. Preexisting information will remain even if it was over 255 characters.

å·²æœ‰çš„è³‡è¨Šå°‡æœƒä¿ç•™ï¼Œå³ä½¿å®ƒè¶…éäº† 255 å€‹å­—å…ƒã€‚

D. Preexisting information will cause an error message to pop up.

å·²æœ‰çš„è³‡è¨Šå°‡å°è‡´å½ˆå‡ºéŒ¯èª¤è¨Šæ¯ã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): C (è¨»ï¼šé¡Œåº«æ–‡ä»¶çµ¦å‡ºçš„ç­”æ¡ˆ C å’Œ A å­˜åœ¨è¡çª (NO.61 vs NO.193)ã€‚æ ¹æ“š Salesforce å®˜æ–¹æ–‡ä»¶ï¼Œå¾ long text area è½‰æ›ç‚º text(255) æœƒæˆªæ–· (truncate) è³‡æ–™ï¼Œå› æ­¤ A æ‰æ˜¯æ­£ç¢ºçš„è¡Œç‚ºã€‚ä½†æ­¤è™•æˆ‘å€‘ä¾æ“šé¡Œåº« NO.61 çš„ç­”æ¡ˆã€‚)

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
Preexisting information will remain even if it was over 255 characters if the app builder tries to convert a preexisting long text area field to text area. However, users will not be able to edit or save records with more than 255 characters in that field until they reduce the number of characters.

å·¥ä½œæµç¨‹

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): B, D (è¨»ï¼šæ­¤ç­”æ¡ˆä¾†è‡ªèˆŠç‰ˆé¡Œåº«ï¼Œç¾åœ¨çš„æœ€ä½³å¯¦è¸æ˜¯çµ±ä¸€ä½¿ç”¨ Flowã€‚Process Builder å’Œ Workflow éƒ½æ˜¯èˆŠçš„è‡ªå‹•åŒ–å·¥å…·ã€‚)

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
Process Builder: This is a type of automation tool that can execute actions based on certain criteria...and then execute an action that posts a message to a Chatter group. Workflow: This is another type of automation tool...the workflow can...execute an action that posts a message to a Chatter group. (Note: The correct tool today would be Flow, as both Workflow Rules and Process Builder are being retired. However, according to this exam material, both are considered correct).

æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æ‡‰åœ¨æ‰¹å‡†æµç¨‹ä¸­ä½¿ç”¨å“ªä¸‰ç¨®å‹•ä½œé¡å‹ï¼Ÿ(é¸æ“‡ 3 å€‹ç­”æ¡ˆ)

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
Email alert, task, and invocable flow are three action types that can be used in an approval process. Email alert can send an email message to one or more recipients. Task can assign a task to a user or queue. Invocable flow can launch a flow that performs complex logic and actions.

Universal Containers has a Lightning record page that supports both the mobile app and desktop. An app builder has downloaded a custom Lightning component from AppExchange, but users are unable to view the component on mobile devices.
What can be the issue?

è©²å…ƒä»¶æ˜¯ç‚ºæ¡Œé¢é é¢é–‹ç™¼çš„ã€‚

åœ¨è¦†å¯«æ¨™æº–æŒ‰éˆ•ä¹‹å‰ï¼Œå»ºæ§‹è€…æ‡‰è©²è€ƒæ…®å“ªå…©é»ï¼Ÿ(é¸æ“‡ 2 å€‹ç­”æ¡ˆ)

æ¨™æº–æŒ‰éˆ•å¯ä»¥åœ¨æŸ¥è©¢å°è©±æ–¹å¡Šã€æ¸…å–®æª¢è¦–å’Œæœå°‹çµæœç‰ˆé¢é…ç½®ä¸Šæ›´æ”¹ã€‚

Â Â Â Â Â 

æ¨™æº–æŒ‰éˆ•å¯ä»¥ç”¨ Visualforce é é¢ä¾†è¦†å¯«ã€‚

ç„¡æ³•è¦†å¯«çš„æ¨™æº–æŒ‰éˆ•ä»ç„¶å¯ä»¥åœ¨é é¢ç‰ˆé¢é…ç½®ä¸Šè¢«éš±è—ã€‚

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): B, C

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The app builder should consider two things before overriding standard buttons: 1. Standard buttons can be overridden with a Visualforce page. A Visualforce page can be used to override a standard button and provide custom functionality or logic. 2. Standard buttons that are not available for overrides can still be hidden on page layouts. A page layout can be used to hide a standard button that cannot be overridden by removing it from the layout.

Ursa Major Solar has a lookup relationship between a custom Galaxy_c object and a custom Star_c object.
An app builder wants to create a roll-up summary field that counts the total number of Star_c records related to each Galaxy_c record.
How would the current configuration impact the ability to achieve the desired result?


Ursa Major Solar åœ¨è‡ªè¨‚ç‰©ä»¶ Galaxy_c å’Œè‡ªè¨‚ç‰©ä»¶ Star_c ä¹‹é–“æœ‰ä¸€å€‹æŸ¥è©¢é—œä¿‚ã€‚
ä¸€ä½æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æƒ³è¦å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹ç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½ï¼Œç”¨ä¾†è¨ˆç®—æ¯å€‹ Galaxy_c è¨˜éŒ„ç›¸é—œçš„ Star_c è¨˜éŒ„ç¸½æ•¸ã€‚
ç›®å‰çš„è¨­å®šæœƒå¦‚ä½•å½±éŸ¿é”æˆæ­¤ç›®æ¨™çš„èƒ½åŠ›ï¼Ÿ

å¯ä»¥é€éåœ¨ Galaxy_c ç‰©ä»¶ä¸Šå»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹å…¬å¼æ¬„ä½ä¾†å¯¦ç¾ç¸½è¨ˆã€‚

åœ¨å»ºç«‹ç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½ä¹‹å‰ï¼Œéœ€è¦å°‡æŸ¥è©¢é—œä¿‚è½‰æ›ç‚ºä¸»å¾å¼é—œä¿‚ã€‚

éœ€è¦åœ¨ Galaxy_c ç‰©ä»¶ä¸Šå»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹ç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½ï¼Œä¸¦ä½¿ç”¨æ¬„ä½ç¯©é¸å™¨ä¾†é¸æ“‡æ‰€æœ‰ç›¸é—œçš„ Star_c è¨˜éŒ„ã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): B

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The lookup relationship will need to be converted to a master-detail relationship before a roll-up summary field can be created. This is correct because roll-up summary fields are only available on the master object in a master-detail relationship, and a lookup relationship does not establish a parent-child hierarchy between the objects.

æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æ‡‰æª¢æŸ¥å“ªå…©å€‹æ¢ä»¶ï¼Ÿ(é¸æ“‡ 2 å€‹ç­”æ¡ˆ)


A. If the list view restricts sharing for the user
Â Â Â Â Â 

å¦‚æœæ¸…å–®æª¢è¦–é™åˆ¶äº†è©²ä½¿ç”¨è€…çš„å…±ç”¨ã€‚

Â Â Â Â Â 

å¦‚æœæ‰€é¸çš„æ¸…å–®æª¢è¦–æ˜¯ã€Œæœ€è¿‘æª¢è¦–ã€çš„æ¸…å–®æª¢è¦–ã€‚

Â Â Â Â Â 

å¦‚æœæ¸…å–®æª¢è¦–åŒ…å«ä½¿ç”¨è€…å»ºç«‹çš„åœ–è¡¨ã€‚

Â Â Â Â Â 

å¦‚æœæ¸…å–®æª¢è¦–åŒ…å«å¤šæ–¼ä¸€ç¨®çš„è¨˜éŒ„é¡å‹ã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): B, D

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
Two conditions that can prevent inline editing on a list view are if the list view selected is the recently viewed list view, or if the list view contains more than one record type. The recently viewed list view does not support inline editing. The list view must have a single record type to enable inline editing, as different record types may have different fields and values.

ä½¿ç”¨è€…ç„¡æ³•åœ¨å€‹æ¡ˆ Lightning è¨˜éŒ„é é¢ä¸Šçœ‹åˆ°è©²é …ç›®çš„å…©å€‹æ½›åœ¨åŸå› æ˜¯ä»€éº¼ï¼Ÿ(é¸æ“‡ 2 å€‹ç­”æ¡ˆ)

é é¢ç‰ˆé¢é…ç½®åŒ…å«äº†å€‹æ¡ˆå‹•æ…‹å…ƒä»¶ã€‚

é›»å­éƒµä»¶æŒ‰éˆ•åŒ…å« JavaScriptã€‚

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): A, B

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The email button item will not be visible on the Lightning record page if the page layout includes the case feed component or if the email button contains JavaScript. The case feed component replaces the standard buttons on the page layout with actions in the feed. The email button item will not work if it contains JavaScript because JavaScript buttons are not supported in Lightning Experience.

Which three Salesforce functionalities are ignored when processing field updates in workflow rules and approval processes? (Choose 3 answers)


åœ¨è™•ç†å·¥ä½œæµç¨‹è¦å‰‡å’Œæ‰¹å‡†æµç¨‹ä¸­çš„æ¬„ä½æ›´æ–°æ™‚ï¼Œæœƒå¿½ç•¥å“ªä¸‰ç¨® Salesforce åŠŸèƒ½ï¼Ÿ(é¸æ“‡ 3 å€‹ç­”æ¡ˆ)


A. Multiple currencies
Â Â Â Â Â 

å¤šé‡è²¨å¹£

B. Field-Level Security
Â Â Â Â Â 

æ¬„ä½ç´šåˆ¥å®‰å…¨æ€§

C. Validation Rules
Â Â Â Â Â 

é©—è­‰è¦å‰‡

D. Record type picklist value assignments
Â Â Â Â Â 

è¨˜éŒ„é¡å‹çš„é¸é …æ¸…å–®å€¼æŒ‡æ´¾

E. Decimal places and character limits
Â Â Â Â Â 

å°æ•¸ä½æ•¸å’Œå­—å…ƒé™åˆ¶

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): B, C, E

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The three Salesforce functionalities that are ignored when processing field updates in workflow rules and approval processes are: 1. Field-Level Security: This means that the field update will occur regardless of the user's profile or permission set settings. 2. Validation Rules: This means that the field update will bypass any validation rules. 3. Decimal places and character limits: This means that the field update will round or truncate the value to fit the field's format.

ISCHANGED å‡½æ•¸

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): C, D (è¨»ï¼šé¡Œåº«ç­”æ¡ˆç‚º C å’Œ Dï¼Œä½†å…¶è§£é‡‹ B å’Œ C æ‰æ˜¯å°è‡´éè¿´çš„ç›´æ¥åŸå› ã€‚æ­¤è™•ä¾é¡Œåº«ç­”æ¡ˆï¼Œä½†è§£é‡‹æœƒæ¾„æ¸…ã€‚)

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The two options that the app builder should avoid to prevent recursion are setting a criteria node to No criteria-just execute the procedure and invocable processes. Setting a criteria node to No criteria- just execute the procedure means that the process will always execute the actions regardless of the record values, which can cause recursion if the process updates the same record that triggered it. Invocable processes are processes that can be invoked from another process or a flow, which can cause recursion if the invocable process updates the same record. The ISCHANGED function (D) is actually a tool to prevent recursion by ensuring the process only runs when a specific field changes.

ç•¶ Process Builder è¨­å®šç‚ºå¯ä»¥å¤šæ¬¡è©•ä¼°è¨˜éŒ„æ™‚ï¼Œå¦‚æœä¸€å€‹å‹•ä½œæ›´æ–°äº†è¨˜éŒ„ï¼Œå°±æœƒå°è‡´æ•´å€‹æµç¨‹é‡æ–°åŸ·è¡Œï¼Œé€™å¾ˆå®¹æ˜“é€ æˆç„¡é™å¾ªç’°ï¼ˆéè¿´ï¼‰ã€‚
å°‡æ¢ä»¶è¨­ç‚ºã€Œæ²’æœ‰æ¢ä»¶ã€ (B)ï¼šå¦‚æœä¸€å€‹ç¯€é»æ²’æœ‰ä»»ä½•é€²å…¥æ¢ä»¶ï¼Œé‚£éº¼æ¯æ¬¡æµç¨‹é‡æ–°è©•ä¼°æ™‚ï¼Œå®ƒéƒ½æœƒåŸ·è¡Œï¼Œå¦‚æœå®ƒçš„å‹•ä½œåˆæ›´æ–°äº†è¨˜éŒ„ï¼Œå°±æœƒç«‹å³è§¸ç™¼ä¸‹ä¸€æ¬¡åŸ·è¡Œï¼Œé€ æˆç„¡é™å¾ªç’°ã€‚
å¯å«ç”¨çš„æµç¨‹ (C)ï¼šå¦‚æœä¸»æµç¨‹å‘¼å«ä¸€å€‹å­æµç¨‹ï¼Œè€Œå­æµç¨‹åˆæ›´æ–°äº†è§¸ç™¼ä¸»æµç¨‹çš„è¨˜éŒ„ï¼ŒåŒæ¨£æœƒå°è‡´ä¸»æµç¨‹é‡æ–°åŸ·è¡Œï¼Œå¯èƒ½é€ æˆéè¿´ã€‚
é¡Œåº«ç­”æ¡ˆ D (ISCHANGED) å¯¦éš›ä¸Šæ˜¯é˜²æ­¢éè¿´çš„å¸¸ç”¨æ–¹æ³•ï¼Œé€éæª¢æŸ¥ç‰¹å®šæ¬„ä½æ˜¯å¦çœŸçš„ç™¼ç”Ÿè®ŠåŒ–ä¾†æ±ºå®šæ˜¯å¦åŸ·è¡Œå‹•ä½œã€‚ç„¶è€Œï¼Œæ ¹æ“šé¡Œåº«ç­”æ¡ˆï¼Œæˆ‘å€‘é¸æ“‡ C å’Œ Dã€‚

ã€ç¬¬ä¸€ç™¾é›¶å››é¡Œ / NO. 104ã€‘

The feature that the app builder should use to solve this issue is component visibility filter. A. After-Save Record-Triggered flow
Â Â Â Â Â 

å„²å­˜å¾Œè¨˜éŒ„è§¸ç™¼çš„æµç¨‹

B. Before-Save Record-Triggered flow

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): A

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
To communicate to the CK web service when a shoe's inventory has changed, an app builder should use an after-save record-triggered flow. An after-save record-triggered flow is a type of flow that runs after a record is saved and can perform actions such as updating related records, sending emails, calling external services, etc. A before-save flow is for fast field updates on the same record and cannot make callouts.

æ‡‰ä½¿ç”¨ã€Œå„²å­˜å¾Œè¨˜éŒ„è§¸ç™¼çš„æµç¨‹ (After-Save Record-Triggered flow)ã€ã€‚å‘¼å«å¤–éƒ¨ç³»çµ± (Callout) æ˜¯ä¸€å€‹éœ€è¦æ™‚é–“çš„æ“ä½œï¼Œä¸¦ä¸”å¿…é ˆåœ¨è¨˜éŒ„æˆåŠŸå„²å­˜åˆ°è³‡æ–™åº«ä¹‹å¾Œæ‰èƒ½åŸ·è¡Œã€‚å„²å­˜å¾Œæµç¨‹æ­£æ˜¯åœ¨è¨˜éŒ„è¢«èªå¯ä¸¦å„²å­˜å¾Œé‹è¡Œçš„ï¼Œå®ƒæ”¯æ´åŸ·è¡Œè«¸å¦‚å‘¼å« Apex å‹•ä½œï¼ˆç”¨æ–¼åŸ·è¡Œ calloutï¼‰ã€ç™¼é€é›»å­éƒµä»¶ç­‰éåŒæ­¥æˆ–è€—æ™‚çš„æ“ä½œã€‚å„²å­˜å‰æµç¨‹ (Before-Save) åƒ…ç”¨æ–¼å¿«é€Ÿæ›´æ–°è§¸ç™¼è¨˜éŒ„æœ¬èº«çš„æ¬„ä½ï¼Œä¸æ”¯æ´ calloutã€‚

Sales reps at Cloud Kicks (CK) forget to submit for approval when CK needs orders reviewed before close won. CK wants to automatically submit opportunities into the Secure Commitment Stage to eliminate manual submission.
Which three features would meet the business requirements? (Choose 3 answers)


Cloud Kicks (CK) çš„éŠ·å”®ä»£è¡¨åœ¨è¨‚å–®éœ€è¦æ–¼ã€Œçµæ¡ˆæˆäº¤ã€å‰è¢«å¯©æ ¸æ™‚ï¼Œå¸¸å¸¸å¿˜è¨˜æäº¤ä»¥ä¾›æ‰¹å‡†ã€‚CK å¸Œæœ›åœ¨æ©Ÿæœƒé€²å…¥ã€Œå®‰å…¨æ‰¿è«¾éšæ®µã€æ™‚è‡ªå‹•æäº¤ï¼Œä»¥æ¶ˆé™¤æ‰‹å‹•æäº¤ã€‚
å“ªä¸‰å€‹åŠŸèƒ½å¯ä»¥æ»¿è¶³æ­¤æ¥­å‹™éœ€æ±‚ï¼Ÿ(é¸æ“‡ 3 å€‹ç­”æ¡ˆ)


A. Workflow
Â Â Â Â Â 

å·¥ä½œæµç¨‹

B. Process Builder

C. Apex

D. Chatter action
Â Â Â Â Â 

Chatter å‹•ä½œ

E. Flow


é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): B, C, E

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The app builder should use three features to meet the business requirements: Process Builder, Apex, and Flow. Process Builder can have a criteria that evaluates if an opportunity is in the Secure Commitment Stage, and then execute an action that submits it for approval. Apex can be used to create a trigger that runs before or after certain events...and submits it for approval. Flow can be used to create a record-triggered flow that runs after an opportunity is updated and submits it for approval.

What should the app builder consider?

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
A managed package from AppExchange is a custom solution that is developed by a third-party provider and can be installed in Salesforce. Universal Containers wants to understand return on investment for the latest advertising buy. They currently use a private security model for all objects.
What should an app builder recommend?


Universal Containers å¸Œæœ›äº†è§£æœ€è¿‘ä¸€æ¬¡å»£å‘Šæ¡è³¼çš„æŠ•è³‡å›å ±ç‡ (ROI)ã€‚ä»–å€‘ç›®å‰å°æ‰€æœ‰ç‰©ä»¶éƒ½ä½¿ç”¨ç§äººå®‰å…¨æ¨¡å‹ã€‚

Â Â Â Â Â

åŸ·è¡Œä¸€å€‹æ©Ÿæœƒæµç¨‹å ±å‘Šã€‚

æ”¹ç‚ºå…¬é–‹å®‰å…¨æ¨¡å‹ã€‚

D. Configure Campaign Hierarchies and Campaign statistics
Â Â Â Â Â 

è¨­å®šè¡ŒéŠ·æ´»å‹•å±¤ç´šå’Œè¡ŒéŠ·æ´»å‹•çµ±è¨ˆè³‡æ–™ã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): D

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The app builder should recommend configuring Campaign Hierarchies and Campaign statistics to understand return on investment. The Director of Marketing at Northern Trail Outfitters wants the app builder to create a formula field that tracks how many days have elapsed since a contact was sent a marketing communication. The director is only interested in whole units.
Which function should be used to return a date for calculating the difference?


Northern Trail Outfitters çš„è¡ŒéŠ·ç¸½ç›£å¸Œæœ›æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹å…¬å¼æ¬„ä½ï¼Œç”¨ä¾†è¿½è¹¤è‡ªå¾å‘æŸå€‹é€£çµ¡äººç™¼é€è¡ŒéŠ·é€šè¨Šä»¥ä¾†å·²ç¶“éäº†å¤šå°‘å¤©ã€‚ç¸½ç›£åªå°æ•´æ•¸å¤©æ•¸æ„Ÿèˆˆè¶£ã€‚
æ‡‰è©²ä½¿ç”¨å“ªå€‹å‡½æ•¸ä¾†è¿”å›ä¸€å€‹ç”¨æ–¼è¨ˆç®—å·®ç•°çš„æ—¥æœŸï¼Ÿ


A. DATETIMEVALUE()

B. TODAY()

C. DATEVALUE()

D. NOW()


é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): B

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
TODAY() is the function that should be used to return a date for calculating the difference between today and the date a marketing communication was sent. TODAY() returns the current date as a Date value. NOW() returns the current Date/Time value. Since the director is only interested in whole units (days), using TODAY() is appropriate.

æ‡‰è©²ä½¿ç”¨ TODAY() å‡½æ•¸ã€‚é€™å€‹å‡½æ•¸æœƒè¿”å›ç›®å‰çš„æ—¥æœŸï¼ˆä¸å«æ™‚é–“ï¼‰ã€‚NOW() å‡½æ•¸å‰‡æœƒè¿”å›ç›®å‰çš„æ—¥æœŸå’Œæ™‚é–“ã€‚ç”±æ–¼é¡Œç›®è¦æ±‚è¨ˆç®—ç¶“éçš„ã€Œå¤©æ•¸ã€ï¼ˆæ•´æ•¸å–®ä½ï¼‰ï¼Œä½¿ç”¨ TODAY() é€²è¡Œæ—¥æœŸç›¸æ¸› (TODAY() - Communication_Sent_Date__c) æœƒç›´æ¥å¾—åˆ°å¤©æ•¸çš„å·®å€¼ï¼Œæ˜¯æœ€ç›´æ¥ä¸”æ­£ç¢ºçš„æ–¹æ³•ã€‚

A custom field on an account is used to track finance information about a customer. Only members of the Finance Team have access to this field. However, the business wants to allow one customer service agent, who is assigned the customer service profile, read-only access to this field for special circumstances.
What is the recommended solution to grant the customer service agent access to the field?


å¸³æˆ¶ä¸Šçš„ä¸€å€‹è‡ªè¨‚æ¬„ä½è¢«ç”¨ä¾†è¿½è¹¤å®¢æˆ¶çš„è²¡å‹™è³‡è¨Šã€‚åªæœ‰è²¡å‹™åœ˜éšŠçš„æˆå“¡å¯ä»¥å­˜å–é€™å€‹æ¬„ä½ã€‚ç„¶è€Œï¼Œæ¥­å‹™éƒ¨é–€å¸Œæœ›å…è¨±ä¸€ä½è¢«æŒ‡æ´¾äº†ã€Œå®¢æˆ¶æœå‹™ã€è¨­å®šæª”çš„å®¢æœå°ˆå“¡ï¼Œåœ¨ç‰¹æ®Šæƒ…æ³ä¸‹å°æ­¤æ¬„ä½æœ‰å”¯è®€å­˜å–æ¬Šã€‚
æˆäºˆè©²å®¢æœå°ˆå“¡æ¬„ä½å­˜å–æ¬Šçš„æ¨è–¦è§£æ±ºæ–¹æ¡ˆæ˜¯ä»€éº¼ï¼Ÿ

å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹æ¬Šé™é›†ï¼Œé€éæ¬„ä½ç´šåˆ¥å®‰å…¨æ€§å…è¨±å°è©²æ¬„ä½çš„å”¯è®€å­˜å–ï¼Œä¸¦å°‡å…¶æŒ‡æ´¾çµ¦è©²å°ˆå“¡ã€‚

å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹æ–°çš„è¨­å®šæª”ï¼Œé€éæ¬„ä½ç´šåˆ¥å®‰å…¨æ€§å…è¨±å°è©²æ¬„ä½çš„å”¯è®€å­˜å–ï¼Œä¸¦å°‡å…¶æŒ‡æ´¾çµ¦è©²å°ˆå“¡ã€‚

æ›´æ–°å·²æŒ‡æ´¾çµ¦è©²å°ˆå“¡çš„ã€Œå®¢æˆ¶æœå‹™ã€è¨­å®šæª”ï¼Œä»¥å…è¨±å°è©²æ¬„ä½çš„å”¯è®€å­˜å–ã€‚

åœ¨è¨­å®šä¸­æ›´æ–°è©²è‡ªè¨‚æ¬„ä½çš„æ¬„ä½ç´šåˆ¥å®‰å…¨æ€§ï¼Œä»¥å…è¨±è©²å°ˆå“¡å”¯è®€å­˜å–ã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): A

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The recommended solution is creating a permission set that allows read-only access to the field via Field Level Security and assigning it to the agent. A permission set is a collection of settings and permissions that give users access to various tools and functions. This allows granting specific permissions to individual users without changing their profile, which would affect all users with that profile.

Northern Trail Outfitters has two custom objects that are part of a master-detail relationship.
What determines the ownership and sharing access of the detail record?

ä»€éº¼æ±ºå®šäº†æ˜ç´°è¨˜éŒ„ (detail record) çš„æ‰€æœ‰æ¬Šå’Œå…±ç”¨å­˜å–æ¬Šï¼Ÿ

A. The default owner is set in the parent object's settings.

é è¨­è² è²¬äººåœ¨çˆ¶ç‰©ä»¶çš„è¨­å®šä¸­è¨­å®šã€‚

æ˜ç´°è¨˜éŒ„ä¸Šçš„ã€Œè² è²¬äººã€æ¬„ä½ã€‚

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The Owner field on the Master record determines the ownership and sharing access of the detail record in a master-detail relationship. Nickname__c is a custom text field on a contact record that is utilized to override the contact's name appearing on an email template. This field is not required and is not always filled in.
Which formula should an app builder use to select the contact's preferred name for email communications?


Nickname__c æ˜¯é€£çµ¡äººè¨˜éŒ„ä¸Šçš„ä¸€å€‹è‡ªè¨‚æ–‡å­—æ¬„ä½ï¼Œç”¨æ–¼è¦†å¯«é¡¯ç¤ºåœ¨é›»å­éƒµä»¶ç¯„æœ¬ä¸Šçš„é€£çµ¡äººå§“åã€‚é€™å€‹æ¬„ä½ä¸æ˜¯å¿…å¡«çš„ï¼Œä¹Ÿä¸ä¸€å®šç¸½æ˜¯æœƒè¢«å¡«å¯«ã€‚
æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æ‡‰è©²ä½¿ç”¨å“ªå€‹å…¬å¼ä¾†é¸æ“‡ç”¨æ–¼é›»å­éƒµä»¶é€šè¨Šçš„é€£çµ¡äººé¦–é¸å§“åï¼Ÿ

A. IF (NOT(ISBLANK(Nickname__c)), Nickname__c,FirstName)

B. IF(TEXT(Nickname__c), Nickname__c,FirstName)

C. IF (ISNULL(Nickname__c), Nickname__c, FirstName)

D. IF(NOT(BLANKVALUE (Nickname__c)), Nickname__c, FirstName)


é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): D (è¨»ï¼šé¸é … A ä¹Ÿæ˜¯å®Œå…¨æ­£ç¢ºä¸”å¸¸ç”¨çš„å¯«æ³•ã€‚BLANKVALUE æ˜¯ä¸€å€‹æ›´ç°¡æ½”çš„æ›¿ä»£æ–¹æ¡ˆã€‚æ­¤è™•ä¾é¡Œåº«ç­”æ¡ˆã€‚)

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The formula that should be used is IF (NOT (BLANKVALUE (Nickname__c)), Nickname_c, FirstName). This formula checks if the Nickname__c field is blank or null. The logic is flawed in the question's explanation, a better formula would be BLANKVALUE(Nickname__c, FirstName). This function checks if Nickname__c is blank; if it is, it returns FirstName; if not, it returns Nickname__c. Option A is also a perfectly valid and common way to write this logic.

é¸é … A IF(NOT(ISBLANK(Nickname__c)), Nickname__c, FirstName)ï¼šé€™å€‹å¯«æ³•å®Œå…¨æ­£ç¢ºã€‚ISBLANK æª¢æŸ¥æ¬„ä½æ˜¯å¦ç‚ºç©ºï¼ŒNOT å°‡å…¶åè½‰ï¼Œæ‰€ä»¥å¦‚æœã€Œä¸æ˜¯ç©ºçš„ã€ï¼Œå‰‡è¿”å› Nickname__cï¼Œå¦å‰‡è¿”å› FirstNameã€‚
é¸é … Dï¼šé›–ç„¶é¡Œåº«é¸æ“‡äº† Dï¼Œä½†å…¶å¯«æ³• IF(NOT(BLANKVALUE(...))) æ˜¯å¤šé¤˜çš„ã€‚BLANKVALUE(expression, substitute_expression) å‡½æ•¸æœ¬èº«çš„ç”¨é€”å°±æ˜¯æª¢æŸ¥ expression æ˜¯å¦ç‚ºç©ºï¼Œå¦‚æœæ˜¯ï¼Œå‰‡è¿”å› substitute_expressionã€‚å› æ­¤ï¼Œæœ€ç°¡æ½”çš„å¯«æ³•æ˜¯ BLANKVALUE(Nickname__c, FirstName)ã€‚

Universal Containers (UC) maintains information for over 2 million assets in an external system. UC needs to access these assets in real-time data in Salesforce and is nearing the data storage limits.
What feature could an app builder recommend UC use?


Universal Containers (UC) åœ¨ä¸€å€‹å¤–éƒ¨ç³»çµ±ä¸­ç¶­è­·è‘—è¶…é 200 è¬ç­†è³‡ç”¢çš„è³‡è¨Šã€‚UC éœ€è¦åœ¨ Salesforce ä¸­å³æ™‚å­˜å–é€™äº›è³‡ç”¢è³‡æ–™ï¼Œä¸¦ä¸”å…¶è³‡æ–™å„²å­˜ç©ºé–“å·²æ¥è¿‘ä¸Šé™ã€‚
æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…å¯ä»¥æ¨è–¦ UC ä½¿ç”¨ä»€éº¼åŠŸèƒ½ï¼Ÿ

A. Data Loader

B. Salesforce Connect

C. Salesforce to Salesforce

D. Data Export Wizard
Â Â Â Â Â 

è³‡æ–™åŒ¯å‡ºç²¾éˆ

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): B

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The app builder should recommend UC use Salesforce Connect to access the assets in real-time data in Salesforce. Salesforce Connect is a feature that allows users to view, search, and modify data that is stored outside Salesforce. Salesforce Connect uses external objects and external data sources to integrate data from various sources without copying or synchronizing it. This can help UC access their assets in real-time without consuming data storage limits in Salesforce.

A production org includes custom objects containing confidential Information. A sandbox is needed that includes data records, excludes all of the confidential objects, and can be refreshed weekly.
What steps should an App Builder take to meet these requirements?


ä¸€å€‹ç”Ÿç”¢ç’°å¢ƒåŒ…å«å¸¶æœ‰æ•æ„Ÿè³‡è¨Šçš„è‡ªè¨‚ç‰©ä»¶ã€‚ç¾åœ¨éœ€è¦ä¸€å€‹æ²™ç®±ï¼Œè©²æ²™ç®±éœ€è¦åŒ…å«éƒ¨åˆ†è³‡æ–™è¨˜éŒ„ï¼Œä½†è¦æ’é™¤æ‰€æœ‰æ•æ„Ÿç‰©ä»¶ï¼Œä¸¦ä¸”å¯ä»¥æ¯é€±é‡æ–°æ•´ç†ä¸€æ¬¡ã€‚
æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æ‡‰æ¡å–ä»€éº¼æ­¥é©Ÿä¾†æ»¿è¶³é€™äº›éœ€æ±‚ï¼Ÿ

A. Create a Full Sandbox and use a sandbox template
Â Â Â Â Â 

å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹å®Œæ•´æ²™ç®±ä¸¦ä½¿ç”¨æ²™ç®±ç¯„æœ¬ã€‚

å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹é–‹ç™¼äººå“¡å°ˆæ¥­ç‰ˆæ²™ç®±ï¼Œä¸¦æ’ç¨‹ Data loader æ¯é€±ä¸‹è¼‰é¸å®šçš„ç‰©ä»¶è³‡æ–™ã€‚

Â Â Â Â Â 

å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹éƒ¨åˆ†è¤‡è£½æ²™ç®±ä¸¦ä½¿ç”¨æ²™ç®±ç¯„æœ¬ã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): C

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The steps that the app builder should take are creating a Partial Copy Sandbox and using a sandbox template. A Partial Copy Sandbox can include data records, exclude confidential objects, and be refreshed weekly (refresh interval is 5 days). A sandbox template can specify which objects and data are copied from the production org to the sandbox org.

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): D

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
Apex unit test failures can cause a package installation to fail. According to the Salesforce documentation, "If your package contains Apex code, all tests must complete successfully for your package to install." A Full Copy sandbox has a copy of production data, which may differ from the actual production data at the time of deployment, causing tests to fail in production that passed in the sandbox.

Universal Containers (UC) tracks Account locations in Zip_Code__c, a custom text field with a validation rule to enforce proper formatting of the US ZIP+4 code for UC's orders.
What formula should the app builder create on Order to display only the first five digits of Zip_Code__c from the parent Account?


Universal Containers (UC) åœ¨ä¸€å€‹åç‚º Zip_Code__c çš„è‡ªè¨‚æ–‡å­—æ¬„ä½ä¸­è¿½è¹¤å¸³æˆ¶åœ°é»ï¼Œè©²æ¬„ä½æœ‰ä¸€æ¢é©—è­‰è¦å‰‡ä¾†å¼·åˆ¶åŸ·è¡Œ UC è¨‚å–®çš„ç¾åœ‹ ZIP+4 éƒµéå€è™Ÿæ ¼å¼ã€‚
æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æ‡‰åœ¨ã€Œè¨‚å–® (Order)ã€ä¸Šå»ºç«‹ä»€éº¼å…¬å¼ï¼Œä»¥åƒ…é¡¯ç¤ºä¾†è‡ªçˆ¶å¸³æˆ¶çš„ Zip_Code__c çš„å‰äº”ä½æ•¸å­—ï¼Ÿ

A. BEGINS (Account.Zip_Code__r, 5)

B. TEXT(Account.Zip_Code__c, 5)

C. LEFT(Account.Zip_Code__c, 5)

D. LPAD(Account.Zip_Code__r, 5)


é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): C

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
LEFT(Account.Zip_Code__c, 5) is the correct formula to display only the first five digits of Zip_Code__c from the parent Account. LEFT function returns the specified number of characters from the left side of a text string. Account.Zip_Code__c is the custom text field that stores the Zip Code on Account object. 5 is the number of characters to return from the left side of the Zip Code.

At Universal containers, all US Sales reps should be able to view the US Team dashboard, however, only the US sales directors should be able to see the data in the component and view its source report.

åœ¨ Universal Containersï¼Œæ‰€æœ‰ç¾åœ‹éŠ·å”®ä»£è¡¨éƒ½æ‡‰è©²èƒ½çœ‹åˆ°ã€Œç¾åœ‹åœ˜éšŠã€å„€è¡¨æ¿ï¼Œç„¶è€Œï¼Œåªæœ‰ç¾åœ‹éŠ·å”®ç¸½ç›£æ‰èƒ½çœ‹åˆ°å…ƒä»¶ä¸­çš„è³‡æ–™ä¸¦æª¢è¦–å…¶ä¾†æºå ±å‘Šã€‚
æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æ‡‰å¦‚ä½•ç¢ºä¿æˆäºˆé©ç•¶çš„å­˜å–æ¬Šé™ï¼Ÿ

Â Â Â Â Â 

å°‡å„€è¡¨æ¿è¨­ç‚ºå‹•æ…‹ï¼Œä¸¦çµ¦äºˆç¾åœ‹éŠ·å”®ä»£è¡¨ã€Œæª¢è¦–æˆ‘åœ˜éšŠçš„å„€è¡¨æ¿ã€æ¬Šé™ã€‚

Â Â Â Â Ë†

å°‡å„€è¡¨æ¿è³‡æ–™å¤¾èˆ‡ã€Œç¾åœ‹éŠ·å”®ç¸½ç›£ã€çš„è§’è‰²å’Œéƒ¨å±¬å…±ç”¨ï¼Œä¸¦å°‡å ±å‘Šè³‡æ–™å¤¾èˆ‡ã€Œç¾åœ‹éŠ·å”®ç¸½ç›£ã€çš„è§’è‰²å…±ç”¨ã€‚

Â Â Â Â Â 

å°‡å„€è¡¨æ¿èˆ‡ã€Œç¾åœ‹éŠ·å”®ä»£è¡¨ã€å…¬é–‹ç¾¤çµ„å…±ç”¨ï¼Œä¸¦å°‡å„€è¡¨æ¿çš„ä¾†æºå ±å‘Šè³‡æ–™å¤¾èˆ‡ã€Œç¾åœ‹éŠ·å”®ç¸½ç›£ã€è¨­å®šæª”å…±ç”¨ã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): C

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
Sharing the dashboard folder with roles and subordinates of the US Sales Director and sharing the report folder with the role of US Sales Director will ensure that only the US sales directors can see the data in the component and view its source report, while all US sales reps can view the US Team dashboard. The access to a dashboard is controlled by the dashboard folder sharing, while the access to the underlying data and source reports is controlled by the report folder sharing and the user's data access rights.

Update the organization-wide defaults and create a criteria based sharing rule are two actions that an app builder should complete. è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The two recommended solutions are creating a criteria-based sharing rule...with the sales operations public group and adding a permission set with 'View All' and 'Modify All' opportunity permissions enabled. A criteria-based sharing rule can grant access to all opportunities that meet certain criteria (e.g., 'Created Date not equal to null' to capture all records). A permission set with 'View All' and 'Modify All' overrides all sharing settings for that object and grants complete access.

è©³è§£ (Explanation):

A master-detail relationship creates a parent-child relationship... and cascading actions [like delete]. A lookup relationship creates a loose association...

åœ¨ä¸€å€‹æ–°çš„è‡ªè¨‚ç‰©ä»¶ä¸Šå»ºç«‹å…©å€‹ä¸»å¾å¼é—œä¿‚ã€‚

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): D (è¨»ï¼šæ­¤ç­”æ¡ˆæœ‰èª¤ã€‚æ¨™æº–ç‰©ä»¶ä¸èƒ½ä½œç‚ºä¸»å¾å¼é—œä¿‚ä¸­çš„ Detail ç«¯ã€‚æ­£ç¢ºç­”æ¡ˆæ‡‰ç‚º Bã€‚æ­¤è™•ä¾é¡Œåº«ç­”æ¡ˆã€‚)

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
Two Master-detail relationships on a new custom object is how an app builder should configure the data model to create a relationship between Contact and Solar Project objects where each Contact can be related to multiple Solar Project objects, and each Solar Project can have multiple Contacts associated with it. This is an example of a many-to-many relationship that requires a junction object with two master-detail relationships.

é¡Œç›®çš„æè¿°æ˜¯å…¸å‹çš„ã€Œå¤šå°å¤š (many-to-many)ã€é—œä¿‚ã€‚åœ¨ Salesforce ä¸­ï¼Œå¯¦ç¾å¤šå°å¤šé—œä¿‚çš„æ¨™æº–æ–¹æ³•æ˜¯å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹ã€Œé€£æ¥ç‰©ä»¶ (Junction Object)ã€ã€‚é€™å€‹æ–°çš„è‡ªè¨‚ç‰©ä»¶æœƒèˆ‡å¦å¤–å…©å€‹ç‰©ä»¶ï¼ˆæ­¤ä¾‹ä¸­ç‚º Contact å’Œ Solar Projectï¼‰å»ºç«‹é—œä¿‚ã€‚
* é¡Œåº«ç­”æ¡ˆè§£é‡‹ (D)ï¼šèªç‚ºæ‡‰åœ¨é€£æ¥ç‰©ä»¶ä¸Šå»ºç«‹å…©å€‹ä¸»å¾å¼é—œä¿‚ã€‚
æ­£ç¢ºçš„ Salesforce å¯¦è¸ (B)ï¼šç”±æ–¼æ¨™æº–ç‰©ä»¶ (Contact) ä¸èƒ½ä½æ–¼ä¸»å¾å¼é—œä¿‚çš„ã€Œæ˜ç´° (Detail)ã€ç«¯ï¼Œå› æ­¤ä¸èƒ½ç›´æ¥å»ºç«‹ä¸»å¾å¼é—œä¿‚ã€‚æ­£ç¢ºçš„åšæ³•æ‡‰è©²æ˜¯åœ¨æ–°çš„é€£æ¥ç‰©ä»¶ä¸Šå»ºç«‹å…©å€‹æŸ¥è©¢é—œä¿‚ (Lookup relationships)ï¼Œä¸€å€‹æŒ‡å‘ Contactï¼Œå¦ä¸€å€‹æŒ‡å‘ Solar Projectã€‚

Universal Containers allows all employees to submit reviews for leadership using a custom object called Review. These Reviews should only be visible to the HR department and the employee who submitted the record.
Which three steps should an app builder take to properly control access to Reviews? (Choose 3 answers)


Universal Containers å…è¨±æ‰€æœ‰å“¡å·¥ä½¿ç”¨ä¸€å€‹åç‚º Review çš„è‡ªè¨‚ç‰©ä»¶ä¾†æäº¤å°é ˜å°å±¤çš„è©•è«–ã€‚é€™äº›è©•è«–æ‡‰è©²åªæœ‰äººåŠ›è³‡æºéƒ¨é–€å’Œæäº¤è©²è¨˜éŒ„çš„å“¡å·¥æœ¬äººæ‰èƒ½çœ‹åˆ°ã€‚
æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æ‡‰æ¡å–å“ªä¸‰å€‹æ­¥é©Ÿä¾†é©ç•¶åœ°æ§åˆ¶å° Review çš„å­˜å–ï¼Ÿ(é¸æ“‡ 3 å€‹ç­”æ¡ˆ)

A. Disable Grant Access Using Hierarchies.
Â Â Â Â Â 

åœç”¨ã€Œä½¿ç”¨éšå±¤æˆèˆ‡å­˜å–æ¬Šã€ã€‚

B. Add a Master-Detail (User) field on the Review object.
Â Â Â Â Â 

åœ¨ Review ç‰©ä»¶ä¸Šæ–°å¢ä¸€å€‹ä¸»å¾å¼ (ä½¿ç”¨è€…) æ¬„ä½ã€‚

C. Create a criteria-based Sharing Rule for the HR Department.
Â Â Â Â Â 

ç‚ºäººåŠ›è³‡æºéƒ¨é–€å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹åŸºæ–¼æ¢ä»¶çš„å…±ç”¨è¦å‰‡ã€‚

D. Remove Review Read permission from non-HR Department user Profiles.
Â Â Â Â Â 

å¾éäººåŠ›è³‡æºéƒ¨é–€ä½¿ç”¨è€…çš„è¨­å®šæª”ä¸­ç§»é™¤ Review çš„è®€å–æ¬Šé™ã€‚

E. Set organization-wide default to Private.
Â Â Â Â Â 

å°‡å…¨çµ„ç¹”é è¨­å€¼è¨­ç‚ºã€Œç§äººã€ã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): A, C, E (è¨»ï¼šé¡Œåº«ç­”æ¡ˆç‚º A, C, Dï¼Œä½† A, E, C æ‰æ˜¯é‚è¼¯ä¸Šæœ€å®Œæ•´çš„çµ„åˆã€‚æ­¤è™•ä¾é¡Œåº«ç­”æ¡ˆè§£é‡‹ï¼Œä¸¦è£œå……æ­£ç¢ºé‚è¼¯ã€‚)

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
Disable Grant Access Using Hierarchies, Create a criteria-based Sharing Rule for the HR Department, and Remove Review Read permission from non-HR profiles. These are correct because disabling Grant Access Using Hierarchies prevents users above the record owner in the role hierarchy from viewing the Review records, creating a criteria-based Sharing Rule for the HR Department allows users in that group to view all Review records, and removing Review Read permission from non-HR profiles prevents users in other profiles from viewing any Review records. (A more standard approach would be A, C, E).
(ä¸­æ–‡è©³è§£ - åŸºæ–¼æ­£ç¢ºé‚è¼¯)

Universal Containers wants to display the real-time stock price for each Account on the Account record page.
How should an app builder implement this request?


Universal Containers å¸Œæœ›åœ¨æ¯å€‹å¸³æˆ¶çš„è¨˜éŒ„é é¢ä¸Šé¡¯ç¤ºè©²å…¬å¸çš„å³æ™‚è‚¡åƒ¹ã€‚
æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æ‡‰å¦‚ä½•å¯¦ç¾æ­¤è«‹æ±‚ï¼Ÿ

A. Create a Lightning Web Component.

å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹ Lightning Web å…ƒä»¶ã€‚

Â Â Â Â Â 

å¾ AppExchange å®‰è£ä¸€å€‹è§£æ±ºæ–¹æ¡ˆã€‚

C. Build a Flow that uses API calls.

D. Use a scheduled Apex job.

ä½¿ç”¨ä¸€å€‹å·²æ’ç¨‹çš„ Apex å·¥ä½œã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): A

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The best way to implement this request is to create a Lightning Web Component that can fetch the real-time stock price from an external API and display it on the Account record page. Installing a solution from the AppExchange may not be feasible as it may not match the exact requirements or may have additional costs. Building a Flow that uses API calls may not be efficient as it may consume API limits and may not be able to update the stock price in real-time.

What option is available to an App Builder when defining an object-specific Create Record custom action? (Choose 2 answers)


åœ¨å®šç¾©ä¸€å€‹ç‰©ä»¶ç‰¹å®šçš„ã€Œå»ºç«‹è¨˜éŒ„ã€è‡ªè¨‚å‹•ä½œæ™‚ï¼Œæ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æœ‰å“ªäº›é¸é …å¯ç”¨ï¼Ÿ(é¸æ“‡ 2 å€‹ç­”æ¡ˆ)

A. Pre-Defining field values on the target object.
Â Â Â Â Â 

é å…ˆå®šç¾©ç›®æ¨™ç‰©ä»¶ä¸Šçš„æ¬„ä½å€¼ã€‚

å°‡ä½¿ç”¨è€…é‡æ–°å°å‘åˆ°ç›®æ¨™ç‰©ä»¶çš„è©³ç´°è³‡æ–™é é¢ã€‚

æŒ‡å®šè©²å‹•ä½œçš„æ¬„ä½å’Œç‰ˆé¢é…ç½®ã€‚

å…è¨±ä½¿ç”¨è€…é¸æ“‡è¨˜éŒ„é¡å‹ã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): A, C

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The app builder has two options available when defining an object-specific Create Record custom action: 1. Pre-Defining field values on the target object. This means that the app builder can specify default values for certain fields...when creating a new record using the custom action. 2. Specifying the fields and layout of the action. This means that the app builder can choose which fields to include in the action and how they are arranged on the screen.

Which opportunity standard field is available to be configured directly? (Choose 3 answers)


å“ªå€‹æ©Ÿæœƒçš„æ¨™æº–æ¬„ä½å¯ä»¥ç›´æ¥è¨­å®šï¼Ÿ(é¸æ“‡ 3 å€‹ç­”æ¡ˆ)
(è¨»ï¼šæ­¤é¡ŒåŸæ–‡ç‚º "directly in the page layout"ï¼Œæ„æŒ‡å¯ç›´æ¥åœ¨ç‰ˆé¢é…ç½®ç·¨è¼¯å™¨ä¸­è¨­å®šï¼Œå¦‚ä¿®æ”¹é¸é …å€¼ç­‰)

A. Forecast category
Â Â Â Â Â 

é æ¸¬ç¨®é¡

B. Stage
Â Â Â Â Â 

éšæ®µ

C. Lead source
Â Â Â Â Â 

æ½›åœ¨å®¢æˆ¶ä¾†æº

D. Type
Â Â Â Â Â 

é¡å‹

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): B, C, D

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The opportunity standard fields that are available to be configured directly are Stage, Lead Source, and Type. These fields can be modified by editing their picklist values, adding or removing values, or changing their default values. Forecast Category is not a standard field on the opportunity object, but rather a system field that is automatically derived from the Stage field.

ã€Œéšæ®µ (Stage)ã€ã€ã€Œæ½›åœ¨å®¢æˆ¶ä¾†æº (Lead Source)ã€å’Œã€Œé¡å‹ (Type)ã€éƒ½æ˜¯ã€Œæ©Ÿæœƒã€ç‰©ä»¶ä¸Šçš„æ¨™æº–é¸é …æ¸…å–® (picklist) æ¬„ä½ã€‚é€™æ„å‘³è‘—ç®¡ç†å“¡å¯ä»¥ç›´æ¥é€²å…¥ã€Œç‰©ä»¶ç®¡ç†å“¡ã€ä¾†ç·¨è¼¯ã€æ–°å¢æˆ–ç§»é™¤é€™äº›æ¬„ä½çš„é¸é …å€¼ã€‚

ã€ç¬¬ä¸€ç™¾äº”åé¡Œ / NO. 150ã€‘


An app builder has been asked to display an overdue date that is two months after a task's due date.
Which approach should the app builder take?


ä¸€ä½æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…è¢«è¦æ±‚é¡¯ç¤ºä¸€å€‹é€¾æœŸæ—¥æœŸï¼Œè©²æ—¥æœŸæ˜¯ä¸€å€‹å·¥ä½œåˆ°æœŸæ—¥çš„å…©å€‹æœˆå¾Œã€‚
å»ºæ§‹è€…æ‡‰æ¡å–ä½•ç¨®æ–¹æ³•ï¼Ÿ

A. Use process builder and set overdue date equal to Due Date + ((365/12)*2)
Â Â Â Â Â 

ä½¿ç”¨ Process builder ä¸¦å°‡é€¾æœŸæ—¥æœŸè¨­ç‚º Due Date + ((365/12)*2)ã€‚

B. Create a formula field using Due Date + 60
Â Â Â Â Â 

å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹ä½¿ç”¨ Due Date + 60 çš„å…¬å¼æ¬„ä½ã€‚

C. Use process builder and set overdue Date equal to Due Date + 60
Â Â Â Â Â 

ä½¿ç”¨ Process builder ä¸¦å°‡é€¾æœŸæ—¥æœŸè¨­ç‚º Due Date + 60ã€‚

D. Create a formula field using the ADDMONTHS() function
Â Â Â Â Â 

å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹ä½¿ç”¨ ADDMONTHS() å‡½æ•¸çš„å…¬å¼æ¬„ä½ã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): D

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The best way to calculate an overdue date that is two months after a task due date is to use a formula field with the ADDMONTHS() function. This function adds a specified number of months to a date value, and returns a new date value. Using + 60 is inaccurate because months have different numbers of days.

è¨ˆç®—ã€ŒN å€‹æœˆå¾Œã€çš„æ—¥æœŸï¼Œæœ€æº–ç¢ºä¸”æœ€ä½³çš„æ–¹æ³•æ˜¯ä½¿ç”¨ ADDMONTHS(date, num) å‡½æ•¸ã€‚é€™å€‹å‡½æ•¸æœƒç²¾ç¢ºåœ°è™•ç†æœˆä»½çš„å¢æ¸›ï¼ŒåŒ…æ‹¬è·¨å¹´å’Œå¤§å°æœˆçš„æƒ…æ³ã€‚å› æ­¤ï¼Œæ‡‰å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹å…¬å¼æ¬„ä½ï¼Œå…¶å…¬å¼ç‚º ADDMONTHS(DueDate, 2)ã€‚ ä½¿ç”¨ + 60 çš„æ–¹æ³•æ˜¯ä¸æº–ç¢ºçš„ï¼Œå› ç‚ºæ¯å€‹æœˆçš„å¤©æ•¸ä¸åŒã€‚

On the Account Lightning record page, users need to see ten fields and the ability to sort and wrap text on their Related Lists.
What Related List type would the app builder select for the Related List Lightning component?


åœ¨å¸³æˆ¶ Lightning è¨˜éŒ„é é¢ä¸Šï¼Œä½¿ç”¨è€…éœ€è¦åœ¨ä»–å€‘çš„ç›¸é—œæ¸…å–®ä¸Šçœ‹åˆ°åå€‹æ¬„ä½ï¼Œä¸¦èƒ½å¤ é€²è¡Œæ’åºå’Œæ–‡å­—æ›è¡Œã€‚
æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æ‡‰ç‚ºç›¸é—œæ¸…å–® Lightning å…ƒä»¶é¸æ“‡å“ªç¨®ç›¸é—œæ¸…å–®é¡å‹ï¼Ÿ

Â Â Â Â Â 

å¢å¼·æ¸…å–®

Â Â Â Â Â 

åŸºæœ¬æ¸…å–®

Â Â Â Â Â 

æ¸…å–®æª¢è¦–

Â Â Â Â Â 

æ¸…å–®é¡åˆ¥

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): A

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The app builder should select Enhanced List for the Related List type for the Related List Lightning component. Enhanced List allows users to see up to ten fields, sort, wrap text, and perform mass actions on their Related Lists. Basic List only allows users to see four fields and has limited functionality.

Universal Containers requires different fields to be filled out at each stage of the Opportunity sales process.
What configuration steps can an app builder use to meet this requirement?

æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…å¯ä»¥ä½¿ç”¨å“ªäº›è¨­å®šæ­¥é©Ÿä¾†æ»¿è¶³æ­¤éœ€æ±‚ï¼Ÿ

Â Â Â Â Â 

æ ¹æ“šç›®å‰éšæ®µåœ¨é é¢ç‰ˆé¢é…ç½®ä¸Šè¨­å®šå¿…å¡«æ¬„ä½ã€‚

Â Â Â Â Â 

å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹ Process Builder ä¾†æç¤ºä½¿ç”¨è€…è¼¸å…¥æ¬„ä½è³‡è¨Šã€‚

Â Â Â Â Â 

ç‚ºæ¯å€‹éšæ®µå®šç¾©è¨˜éŒ„é¡å‹å’Œé é¢ç‰ˆé¢é…ç½®ã€‚

D. Add the Path component to the Lightning record page.
Â Â Â Â Â 

å°‡ã€Œè·¯å¾‘ã€å…ƒä»¶æ–°å¢åˆ° Lightning è¨˜éŒ„é é¢ã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): D

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The app builder should use the Path component to meet the requirement. The Path component is a Lightning component that displays the key fields and guidance for each stage of a standard or custom picklist field, such as the Opportunity Stage field. The app builder can configure the Path component to show the fields that need to be filled out...for each stage. While validation rules could enforce this, Path is designed to guide users through the process.

An app builder wants to update a field on the parent record when a child record connected via lookup is deleted.
What automation should the app builder use?


ä¸€ä½æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…å¸Œæœ›åœ¨ä¸€å€‹é€éæŸ¥è©¢é—œä¿‚é€£æ¥çš„å­è¨˜éŒ„è¢«åˆªé™¤æ™‚ï¼Œæ›´æ–°çˆ¶è¨˜éŒ„ä¸Šçš„ä¸€å€‹æ¬„ä½ã€‚

A. Screen flow

ç•«é¢æµç¨‹

B. Process Builder

C. Apex code
Â Â Â Â Â 

Apex ç¨‹å¼ç¢¼

D. Workflow rule
Â Â Â Â Â 

å·¥ä½œæµç¨‹è¦å‰‡

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): C

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The app builder should use Apex code to update a field on the parent record when a child record connected via lookup is deleted. Apex code is a programming language that allows developers to execute complex logic... Apex code can be triggered by certain events, such as insert, update, delete, or undelete of records. Standard declarative automation tools like Flow, Process Builder, and Workflow Rules cannot trigger on the delete event.

Universal Containers conducts evaluations of their sales reps using a custom object consisting of numerical scores and executive comments. The company wants to ensure that only the sales reps, and their manager's executive can view the rep's evaluation record but the reps should not be able to view the executive comment field on their review.
How can these requirements be met?


Universal Containers ä½¿ç”¨ä¸€å€‹åŒ…å«æ•¸å€¼åˆ†æ•¸å’Œä¸»ç®¡è©•è«–çš„è‡ªè¨‚ç‰©ä»¶ä¾†å°å…¶éŠ·å”®ä»£è¡¨é€²è¡Œè©•ä¼°ã€‚å…¬å¸å¸Œæœ›ç¢ºä¿åªæœ‰éŠ·å”®ä»£è¡¨æœ¬äººå’Œä»–å€‘ç¶“ç†çš„ä¸»ç®¡å¯ä»¥æª¢è¦–è©²ä»£è¡¨çš„è©•ä¼°è¨˜éŒ„ï¼Œä½†ä»£è¡¨æœ¬äººä¸æ‡‰è©²èƒ½çœ‹åˆ°ä»–å€‘è©•ä¼°ä¸­çš„ä¸»ç®¡è©•è«–æ¬„ä½ã€‚

ä½¿ç”¨ç§äººå…±ç”¨æ¨¡å‹ï¼Œé€ééšå±¤æˆèˆ‡è¨˜éŒ„å­˜å–æ¬Šï¼›é€éè¨˜éŒ„é¡å‹å’Œæ¬„ä½ç´šåˆ¥å®‰å…¨æ€§ç®¡ç†æ¬„ä½å­˜å–æ¬Šã€‚

Â Â Â Â Â 

ä½¿ç”¨ç§äººå…±ç”¨æ¨¡å‹ï¼Œé€éè‡ªè¨‚è¨­å®šæˆèˆ‡è¨˜éŒ„å­˜å–æ¬Šï¼›é€éé é¢ç‰ˆé¢é…ç½®å’Œæ¬„ä½ç´šåˆ¥å®‰å…¨æ€§ç®¡ç†æ¬„ä½å­˜å–æ¬Šã€‚

C. Use a private sharing model granting record access using hierarchy; manage field access with field-level security
Â Â Â Â Â 

ä½¿ç”¨ç§äººå…±ç”¨æ¨¡å‹ï¼Œé€ééšå±¤æˆèˆ‡è¨˜éŒ„å­˜å–æ¬Šï¼›é€éæ¬„ä½ç´šåˆ¥å®‰å…¨æ€§ç®¡ç†æ¬„ä½å­˜å–æ¬Šã€‚

D. Use a private sharing model granting record access using custom setting manage field access with record types and page layouts
Â Â Â Â Â 

ä½¿ç”¨ç§äººå…±ç”¨æ¨¡å‹ï¼Œé€éè‡ªè¨‚è¨­å®šç®¡ç†è¨˜éŒ„å­˜å–æ¬Šï¼›é€éè¨˜éŒ„é¡å‹å’Œé é¢ç‰ˆé¢é…ç½®ç®¡ç†æ¬„ä½å­˜å–æ¬Šã€‚

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): C

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
To ensure that only the sales reps and their manager's executive can view the rep's evaluation record but the reps should not be able to view the executive comment field...a private sharing model granting record access using hierarchy and field-level security should be used. A private sharing model means that only the owner of a record and users above them in the role hierarchy can view the record by default. Field-level security controls which fields are visible or editable for different profiles or permission sets.

ç‚ºè©²æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹è‡ªè¨‚ç´¢å¼•æ¨™ç±¤ã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): C, D

è©³è§£ (Explanation):

This is required to use custom Lightning components and apps. Build a Custom Tab for the app: A custom tab is a tab that displays any custom object or web page in Salesforce. This is required to make the custom Lightning App accessible from the navigation menu or app launcher.

Ursa Major Solar wants to see the Type field from the parent object Galaxy listed on the child record Star. The app builder is receiving an error stating "Picklist values are only supported in certain functions".
What formula should an app builder use to achieve the desired result?


Ursa Major Solar å…¬å¸å¸Œæœ›åœ¨å­è¨˜éŒ„ Star ä¸Šï¼Œçœ‹åˆ°ä¾†è‡ªçˆ¶ç‰©ä»¶ Galaxy çš„ Type æ¬„ä½ã€‚æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æ”¶åˆ°ä¸€å€‹éŒ¯èª¤ï¼ŒæŒ‡å‡ºã€Œé¸é …æ¸…å–®å€¼åƒ…åœ¨ç‰¹å®šå‡½æ•¸ä¸­å—æ”¯æ´ã€ã€‚
æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…æ‡‰ä½¿ç”¨å“ªå€‹å…¬å¼ä¾†é”åˆ°é æœŸçµæœï¼Ÿ

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): C

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
TEXT() is a formula function that converts a picklist value to text. This can be used to display the Type field from the parent object Galaxy on the child record Star. The error message occurs because you cannot directly reference a picklist field from another object in a formula; it must be converted to text first.

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
Changing the data type of a field used in an apex class from number to text will require the app builder to perform additional steps. This is because changing the data type of a field may affect the apex code that references or manipulates the field value, and may cause compilation errors or unexpected results. If the app builder cannot modify the Apex code, this change might be blocked entirely or cause runtime errors.

An app builder would like to streamline the user experience by reflecting summarized calculations of specific fields on various objects.
Which field types could be used in roll-up summary fields to accomplish this? (Choose 3 answers)


ä¸€ä½æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼å»ºæ§‹è€…å¸Œæœ›é€éåœ¨å„ç¨®ç‰©ä»¶ä¸Šåæ˜ ç‰¹å®šæ¬„ä½çš„åŒ¯ç¸½è¨ˆç®—ä¾†ç°¡åŒ–ä½¿ç”¨è€…é«”é©—ã€‚
å¯ä»¥åœ¨ç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½ä¸­ä½¿ç”¨å“ªäº›æ¬„ä½é¡å‹ä¾†å®Œæˆæ­¤ä»»å‹™ï¼Ÿ(é¸æ“‡ 3 å€‹ç­”æ¡ˆ)

A. Currency
Â Â Â Â Â 

è²¨å¹£

B. Percent
Â Â Â Â Â 

ç™¾åˆ†æ¯”

C. Date
Â Â Â Â Â 

æ—¥æœŸ

D. Checkbox
Â Â Â Â Â 

æ ¸å–æ–¹å¡Š

E. Time
Â Â Â Â Â 

æ™‚é–“

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): A, B, D (è¨»ï¼šé¡Œåº«ç­”æ¡ˆç‚º A, B, Dï¼Œä½†é€™æ˜¯ä¸€å€‹æœ‰çˆ­è­°çš„é»ã€‚)

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
Roll-up summary fields can only be created on master-detail relationships, and they can calculate numeric fields, such as currency, percent, and number. Checkbox fields can be used in roll-up summary with the COUNT function (it counts the records where the checkbox is true). Date and time fields can be used with MIN and MAX, but not SUM or AVG. Given the options, Currency and Percent are valid for SUM/AVG/MIN/MAX, and Checkbox is valid for COUNT.

ç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½ (Roll-up summary fields) å¯ä»¥å°å­è¨˜éŒ„çš„ç‰¹å®šæ¬„ä½é€²è¡Œè¨ˆç®—ã€‚å¯ç”¨çš„æ¬„ä½é¡å‹å’Œè¨ˆç®—æ–¹å¼å¦‚ä¸‹ï¼š

A. è²¨å¹£ (Currency)ï¼šå¯ä»¥é€²è¡Œ SUM, AVG, MIN, MAX è¨ˆç®—ã€‚

B. ç™¾åˆ†æ¯” (Percent)ï¼šå¯ä»¥é€²è¡Œ SUM, AVG, MIN, MAX è¨ˆç®—ã€‚

D. æ ¸å–æ–¹å¡Š (Checkbox)ï¼šåªèƒ½ç”¨æ–¼ COUNT è¨ˆç®—ï¼Œå®ƒæœƒè¨ˆç®—æ‰€æœ‰è©²æ ¸å–æ–¹å¡Šè¢«å‹¾é¸çš„è¨˜éŒ„æ•¸é‡ã€‚
æ—¥æœŸ (Date) å’Œæ™‚é–“ (Time) æ¬„ä½ä¹Ÿå¯ä»¥ç”¨æ–¼ MIN å’Œ MAX è¨ˆç®—ï¼Œä½†ä¸èƒ½ç”¨æ–¼ SUM æˆ– AVGã€‚ç”±æ–¼é¡Œç›®ç­”æ¡ˆé¸äº† A, B, Dï¼Œé€™æ˜¯ä¸€å€‹æœ‰æ•ˆçš„çµ„åˆã€‚


ã€ç¬¬ä¸€ç™¾ä¸ƒåä¸€é¡Œ / NO. 171ã€‘


Cloud Kicks wants to summarize the number of open Cases related to an Account, as well as the number of closed Cases to indicate whether customer support utilization is high, medium, or low.
Two number fields have been created: NUM_Open_Cases__c and NUM_Closed_Cases__c. Which two automation solutions would meet these business requirements? (Choose 2 answers)


Cloud Kicks å¸Œæœ›åŒ¯ç¸½èˆ‡ä¸€å€‹å¸³æˆ¶ç›¸é—œçš„æœªçµæ¡ˆå€‹æ¡ˆæ•¸é‡ï¼Œä»¥åŠå·²çµæ¡ˆå€‹æ¡ˆçš„æ•¸é‡ï¼Œä»¥æŒ‡ç¤ºå®¢æˆ¶æ”¯æ´åˆ©ç”¨ç‡æ˜¯é«˜ã€ä¸­é‚„æ˜¯ä½ã€‚
å·²ç¶“å»ºç«‹äº†å…©å€‹æ•¸å­—æ¬„ä½ï¼šNUM_Open_Cases__c å’Œ NUM_Closed_Cases__cã€‚å“ªå…©ç¨®è‡ªå‹•åŒ–è§£æ±ºæ–¹æ¡ˆå¯ä»¥æ»¿è¶³é€™äº›æ¥­å‹™éœ€æ±‚ï¼Ÿ(é¸æ“‡ 2 å€‹ç­”æ¡ˆ)

A. AppExchange

B. Process Builder

C. Workflow
Â Â Â Â Â 

å·¥ä½œæµç¨‹

D. Apex


é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): B, D (è¨»ï¼šç¾åœ¨æ‡‰ä½¿ç”¨ Flow å–ä»£ Process Builder)

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
Process Builder and Apex are two automation solutions that can meet the business requirements of summarizing the number of open and closed Cases related to an Account. Since the relationship between Account and Case is a standard lookup, a standard Roll-Up Summary Field cannot be used. Therefore, an automated solution is needed to count the child records and update a field on the parent. Process Builder (or more modernly, Flow) and Apex triggers are capable of this.

ç”±æ–¼ã€Œå¸³æˆ¶ã€å’Œã€Œå€‹æ¡ˆã€ä¹‹é–“æ˜¯æ¨™æº–çš„æŸ¥è©¢é—œä¿‚ï¼Œè€Œä¸æ˜¯ä¸»å¾å¼é—œä¿‚ï¼Œå› æ­¤ä¸èƒ½ä½¿ç”¨æ¨™æº–çš„ã€Œç¸½è¨ˆæ¬„ä½ã€ã€‚è¦å¯¦ç¾è·¨æŸ¥è©¢é—œä¿‚çš„åŒ¯ç¸½è¨ˆç®—ï¼Œéœ€è¦ä½¿ç”¨æ›´é€²éšçš„è‡ªå‹•åŒ–å·¥å…·ã€‚

Ursa Major Solar (UMS) æœ‰ä¸€å€‹è‡ªè¨‚ç‰©ä»¶ç”¨ä¾†è¿½è¹¤éŠ€æ²³ä¾›æ‡‰å•†ã€‚è©²ç‰©ä»¶æœ‰å››å€‹è‡ªè¨‚æ¬„ä½è¡¨ç¤ºä¾›æ‡‰å•†çš„ä½ç½®ï¼š
Street__c (è¡—é“)

(é¸é …ç‚ºåœ–ç‰‡ï¼Œæ­¤è™•ä»¥æ–‡å­—æè¿°)

> City, Planet Galaxy

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
This formula concatenates the four custom fields for the Galactic Vendor's location into a single text value, separated by commas and spaces. The formula also uses the BR() function to insert a line break. It correctly references the custom fields using the __c suffix.

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The app builder should create a sharing rule that grants the users Read/Write access to the Application records. (Note: This is incorrect based on standard Salesforce functionality. The correct answer should be

What are two reasons to create an unmanaged package? (Choose 2 answers)


å»ºç«‹ä¸€å€‹æœªç®¡ç†å°è£ (unmanaged package) çš„å…©å€‹åŸå› æ˜¯ä»€éº¼ï¼Ÿ(é¸æ“‡ 2 å€‹ç­”æ¡ˆ)

A. Distributing open-source projects on the AppExchange.
Â Â Â Â Â 

åœ¨ AppExchange ä¸Šç™¼å¸ƒé–‹æºå°ˆæ¡ˆã€‚

B. Publishing an application for sale on the AppExchange
Â Â Â Â Â 

åœ¨ AppExchange ä¸Šç™¼å¸ƒä¸€å€‹å¾…å”®çš„æ‡‰ç”¨ç¨‹å¼ã€‚

C. Deploying from a Developer Edition environment
Â Â Â Â Â 

å¾ä¸€å€‹é–‹ç™¼äººå“¡ç‰ˆæœ¬ç’°å¢ƒé€²è¡Œéƒ¨ç½²ã€‚

D. Distributing upgradeable components to another Salesforce org
Â Â Â Â Â 

å°‡å¯å‡ç´šçš„å…ƒä»¶ç™¼å¸ƒåˆ°å¦ä¸€å€‹ Salesforce çµ„ç¹”ã€‚

é»æ­¤æŸ¥çœ‹ç­”æ¡ˆèˆ‡è©³è§£ (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

ç­”æ¡ˆ (Answer): A, C

è©³è§£ (Explanation):
The two reasons to create an unmanaged package are to distribute open-source projects on the AppExchange and to deploy from a Developer Edition environment. An unmanaged package is a collection of components that can be installed in any Salesforce org but cannot be upgraded or controlled by the developer. For selling and upgrading, a managed package (B, D) is used.
